OBJECT Table 37 Sales Line
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=03/20/26;
    Time=[ 2:03:43 PM];
    Version List=NAVW1.x,N.7.2.1;

  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnInsert=VAR
               VehicleOwnOptL@1109400002 : Record 5045386;
               VehicleOwnOpt2L@1109400001 : Record 5045386;
               VehicleL@1109400000 : Record 5025400;
               SalesLineL@1109400003 : Record 37;
             BEGIN
               // Start PA032225
               IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnInsert,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'') THEN
                 EXIT;
               // Stop PA032225

               // Start PA033019
               CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Insert);
               // Stop PA033019
               LOCKTABLE;
               // Start PA034053.I000514
               GetSalesHeader();
               // Stop PA034053.I000514
               // Start INC
               IF ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::Service) AND (Type = Type::"Charge (Item)") AND
                  ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Credit Memo","Document Type"::Invoice])
               THEN
                 ERROR(C_INC080,"Document Type");
               StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);
               SalesHeader."No." := '';
               SalesLineL.RESET;
               SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
               SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
               SalesLineL.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<>%1',"Line No.");
               SalesLineL.SETFILTER("Order Type",'<>%1',SalesHeader."Order Type");
               // Start PA036650
               IF NOT SalesLineL.ISEMPTY THEN
               // Stop PA036650
                 SalesLineL.DELETEALL;
               "Order Type" := SalesHeader."Order Type";
               "Customer Group Code" := SalesHeader."Customer Group Code";
               "Dealer Code" := SalesHeader."Dealer Code";
               // Stop INC
               IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
                 "Vehicle Unit Price Date" := SalesHeader."Vehicle Unit Price Date";
               CheckExclusiveDiffTax();
               // Start PA042665
               CheckEmmisionLegalTxt();
               // Stop PA042665
               // Start PA035176
               IF NOT (("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND
                  ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Credit Memo","Document Type"::"Return Order"]) AND
               // Start EU.0139128.139973
                  ((SalesHeader."Applies-to Doc. No." <> '') OR ("Appl.-from Item Entry" <> 0)))
               // Stop EU.0139128.139973
               THEN
               // Stop PA035176
                 IF ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND ("No." <> '') THEN BEGIN
                   VALIDATE(Quantity,1);
                   VehicleUnitG.MakeSalLineOption(Rec);
                   IF VIN <> '' THEN
                     GetOptionPrice();
                   SalesPriceCalculation();
                 END;
               // Start EU.0032221
               IF ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND
                  ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Order) AND
                  ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Own Option") AND
                  (Item."Make Code" = '')
               THEN BEGIN
                 VALIDATE("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code", SalesHeader."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
               END;
               // Stop EU.0032221

               IF ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND ("Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND
               // Start INC
                  (Type <> Type::" ") AND (VIN = '') AND (Type <> Type::"Charge (Item)")
               // Stop INC
               // Start PA039974
               THEN
                 IF NOT "System-Created Entry" THEN BEGIN
                   SalesLine2.RESET;
                   SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
                   SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
                   SalesLine2.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<%1',"Line No.");
                   SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Item Type","Item Type"::Vehicle);
                   SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Order Type","Order Type");
                   SalesLine2.SETFILTER(VIN,'>%1','');
                   IF SalesLine2.FINDLAST THEN
                     IF VehicleG.GET(SalesLine2.VIN) THEN
                        VALIDATE(VIN, SalesLine2.VIN);
                 END;
               // Stop PA039974
               "Disable for Requisition" := SalesHeader."Disable for Requisition";
               VALIDATE("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
               CheckBelongingLines;
               // Start INC
               IF ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Quote,"Document Type"::Order,"Document Type"::Invoice]) AND
                  ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND
                  ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Own Option") AND
                  ("No." <> '')
               THEN BEGIN
                 IF VehicleL.GET(VIN) THEN BEGIN
                   VehicleOwnOptL.RESET;
                   VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);
                   VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Option Code","No.");
                   VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Book No.",VehicleL."Current Book No.");
                   VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Sales Order No.","Document No.");
                   VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Sales Order Line No.","Line No.");
               // Start PA036650
                   IF VehicleOwnOptL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
               // Stop PA036650
                     VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Sales Order No.",'');
                     VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Sales Order Line No.",0);
                     IF VehicleOwnOptL.FINDFIRST AND (VehicleOwnOptL.COUNT = 1) THEN BEGIN
                       VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Order No." := "Document No.";
                       VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Order Line No." := "Line No.";
                       IF (VehicleOwnOptL."Serial No." <> '') AND (VehicleOwnOptL."Service Order No." <> '') THEN
                         "Serial No." := VehicleOwnOptL."Serial No."
                       ELSE
                         VehicleOwnOptL."Serial No." := "Serial No.";
                       Description := VehicleOwnOptL.Description;
                       "Description 2":= VehicleOwnOptL."Description 2";
                       "Veh. Opt. Line No." := VehicleOwnOptL."Option Line No.";
                       VehicleOwnOptL.MODIFY(TRUE);
                     END ELSE BEGIN
                       CLEAR(VehicleOwnOptL);
                       VehicleOwnOptL.INIT;
                       VehicleOwnOptL.VIN := VIN;
                       VehicleOwnOptL."Option Code" := "No.";
                       VehicleOwnOptL."Book No." := VehicleL."Current Book No.";
                       VehicleOwnOpt2L.RESET;
                       VehicleOwnOpt2L.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);
                       VehicleOwnOpt2L.SETRANGE("Option Code","No.");
                       VehicleOwnOpt2L.SETRANGE("Book No.",VehicleL."Current Book No.");
                       IF VehicleOwnOpt2L.FINDLAST THEN
                         VehicleOwnOptL."Line No." := VehicleOwnOpt2L."Line No." + 10000
                       ELSE
                         VehicleOwnOptL."Line No." := 10000;
                       VehicleOwnOptL."Serial No." := "Serial No.";
                       VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Order No." := "Document No.";
                       VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Order Line No." := "Line No.";
                       VehicleOwnOptL.Description := Description;
                       VehicleOwnOptL."Description 2" := "Description 2";
                       VehicleOwnOptL.INSERT(TRUE);
                     END;
                   END;
                 END;
               END;
               // Stop INC
               // Start EU.0000048
               // Start EU.0007737.7676
               IF ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases") AND
                  (Type IN [Type::"Account (G/L)", Type::Item, Type::Resource, Type::"Charge (Item)"])
               THEN
               // Stop EU.0007737.7676
               // Start EU.0007737.7677
                 IF SalesHeader."Your Reference" > '' THEN BEGIN
                   IF "Your Reference" = '' THEN
                     "Your Reference" := SalesHeader."Your Reference";
               // Start EU.0054640
               // Stop EU.0054640
                 END;
               // Stop EU.0007737.7677
               // Stop EU.0000048
               // Start PA033985.19040
               // Stop PA033985.19040
               // Start PA038126
               TempVehDispPurchG.UpdateLinesFromSalesLine(Rec,FALSE);
               // Stop PA038126
               // Start PA032225

               // Start EU.0056707
               IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Order) AND
                  ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases") AND
                  (Type = Type::Item)
               THEN BEGIN
                 "Tour Code" := SalesHeader."Tour Code";
               END;
               // Stop EU.0056707
               // Start EU.0158119.158623
               IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Order) AND ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases") THEN
                 IF Type <> Type::" " THEN
                   TESTFIELD("No.");
               // Stop EU.0158119.158623
               ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnInsert,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'');
               // Stop PA032225
             END;

    OnModify=VAR
               ExRecordL@3245300 : Record 37;
             BEGIN
               // Start PA032225
               IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnModify,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'') THEN
                 EXIT;
               // Stop PA032225

               // Start PA039250
               StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);
               // Stop PA039250
               // Start PA033019
               CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Modify);
               // Stop PA033019
               // Start INC
               IF IsImporter THEN BEGIN
                 DealerMgmtG.SalesLineCheckStatus(Rec);
                 IF NOT SalesLineUpdateG THEN BEGIN
                   UserSetupGet();
                   IF NOT UserSetupG."Edit Pick in Progress" THEN
                     TESTFIELD("Picking in Progress",FALSE);
                 END;
               END;
               // Start INC
               IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
                 IF "Item Type" IN [
                    "Item Type"::Item,
                    "Item Type"::"G/L Account",
                    "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer",
                    "Item Type"::"Own Option"]
               THEN BEGIN
                 VehOptionInvG.RESET;
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
                 IF VehOptionInvG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                   VehOptionInvG.CALCFIELDS("Available in Separate Invoice","Avail. in Separate Posted Inv.");
                   IF (VehOptionInvG."Available in Separate Invoice") OR (VehOptionInvG."Avail. in Separate Posted Inv.") THEN
                     ERROR(C_INC066);
                 END;
               END;

               IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Blanket Order") AND
                  ((Type <> xRec.Type) OR ("No." <> xRec."No."))
               THEN BEGIN
                 SalesLine2.RESET;
                 SalesLine2.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Blanket Order No.","Blanket Order Line No.");
                 SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Blanket Order No.","Document No.");
                 SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Blanket Order Line No.","Line No.");
                 IF SalesLine2.FINDSET THEN
                   REPEAT
                     SalesLine2.TESTFIELD(Type,Type);
                     SalesLine2.TESTFIELD("No.","No.");
                   UNTIL SalesLine2.NEXT = 0;
               END;
               // Start INC
               IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
                 IF ("VAT %" <> xRec."VAT %") OR ("VAT Calculation Type" <> xRec."VAT Calculation Type") THEN BEGIN
                   OptionVariantG.RESET;
               // Start EU.0169755.165049
                   OptionVariantG.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.","Document Line No.","Document Type",Area);
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Area,OptionVariantG.Area::Sale);
               // Stop EU.0169755.165049
                   OptionVariantG.SetVat(OptionVariantG, "VAT %", "VAT Calculation Type");
                 END;
               // Stop INC
               // Start PA044975
               IF "Process Type" = "Process Type"::Manually THEN
                 ReservMgt.SalesLineVerifyChange(Rec);
               // Stop PA044975
               // Start EU.0032453
               IF NOT ExRecordL.GET("Document Type", "Document No.", "Line No.") THEN
                 ExRecordL.INIT;
               // Start EU.0098776
               IF (ExRecordL."No." = '') OR (ExRecordL."No." = "No.") THEN
                 ShoppingCartMgtG.WriteSalesLineQuantityModificationLostSaleData(
                   Rec, (Quantity - ExRecordL.Quantity), (Amount - ExRecordL.Amount), ("Amount Including VAT" - ExRecordL."Amount Including VAT"));
               // Stop EU.0098776
               // Stop EU.0032453
               // Start PA034053.I000514
               IF GetSalesHeader() THEN
               // Stop PA034053.I000514
                 VALIDATE("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
               CheckBelongingLines;
               // Start PA033985.19040
               // Stop PA033985.19040
               // Start PA038126
               // Start EU.0090125
               MODIFY;
               FindStatus(FALSE);
               // Stop EU.0090125
               // Start EU.0089120
               IF (xRec.VIN <> VIN) AND (xRec.VIN <> '') THEN
                 TempVehDispPurchG.UpdateLinesFromSalesLine(xRec, TRUE);
               // Stop EU.0089120
               TempVehDispPurchG.UpdateLinesFromSalesLine(Rec,FALSE);
               // Stop PA038126
               // Start PA032225
               ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnModify,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'');
               // Stop PA032225
             END;

    OnDelete=VAR
               VehOrderHdrL@1109400000 : Record 36;
               VehOrderLineL@1109400001 : Record 37;
               VehicleOwnOptL@1109400004 : Record 5045386;
               VehicleL@1109400005 : Record 5025400;
               SalesLineL@1109400006 : Record 37;
               VehLedgEntryL@1101194985 : Record 5025405;
               DealerVehReqStatusL@1055601 : Record 5086716;
               NotOwnedVehicleL@1109400007 : Record 5205936;
               TechDataValueL@1109400008 : Record 5205856;
               SalesLineTempL@9877600 : TEMPORARY Record 37;
               NextLineNoL@1109400002 : Integer;
               LineExistsL@1109400003 : Boolean;
               OutstandingAmtWithoutTaxL@9877601 : Decimal;
             BEGIN
               // Start PA032225
               IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnDelete,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'') THEN
                 EXIT;
               // Stop PA032225

               // Start PA039250
               StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);
               // Stop PA039250
               // Start PA033019
               CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Delete);
               // Stop PA033019
               // Start INC
               IF "Shipment No." = '' THEN
                 TESTFIELD("Qty. Shipped Not Invoiced",0);
               IF "Return Receipt No." = '' THEN
                 TESTFIELD("Return Qty. Rcd. Not Invd.",0);

               TESTFIELD("Reserved Qty. (Base)",0);
               IF "Purch. Order Line No." <> 0 THEN
                 ERROR(
                   Text000,
                   "Purchase Order No.");

               IF IsImporter THEN BEGIN
                 DealerMgmtG.SalesLineCheckStatus(Rec);
                 IF ("Document Type"IN ["Document Type"::Quote,"Document Type"::Order]) AND
                    ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND
                    ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle)
                 THEN BEGIN
                   VehicleStocklistG.RESET;
                   VehicleStocklistG.SETCURRENTKEY("Dealer Sales Order No.",VIN);
                   VehicleStocklistG.SETRANGE("Dealer Sales Order No.","Document No.");
                   VehicleStocklistG.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);
               // Start PA036650
                   IF VehicleStocklistG.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
               // Stop PA036650
                     REPEAT
                       VehicleStocklistG.VALIDATE("Dealer Sales Order No.",'');
               // Start PA042493
               // Start PA042825
                       VehicleStocklistG.UpdateStatus(DealerVehReqStatusL, VehicleStocklistG."Dealer Request Status"::Available, '' ,'' , 0, '', '', 0D, '', '', '', 0D, '');
               // Stop PA042825
               // Stop PA042493
                       VehicleStocklistG.MODIFY;
                     UNTIL VehicleStocklistG.NEXT = 0;
                 END;
               // Start IMS25007
                 IF DealerMgmtG.GetDealer() <> '' THEN BEGIN
                   GetSalesHeader();
                   IF SalesHeader."Document Type" = SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN
                     IF "Item Type" IN ["Item Type"::"Own Option","Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer"] THEN
                       ERROR(C_IMS011,"Item Type");
                 END;
               // Stop IMS25007
               END;
               StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);
               // Start PA032071
               // Stop PA032071
               IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
                 VehOptionInvG.RESET;
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
                 IF VehOptionInvG.FINDSET THEN
                   REPEAT
                     VehOptionInvG.CALCFIELDS("Available in Separate Invoice","Avail. in Separate Posted Inv.");
                     IF VehOptionInvG."Available in Separate Invoice" THEN
                       ERROR(C_INC065,VIN);
                     IF (VehOptionInvG."Avail. in Separate Posted Inv.") AND ("Quantity Invoiced" <> Quantity) THEN
                       ERROR(C_INC065,VIN);
                   UNTIL VehOptionInvG.NEXT = 0;
               END;
               IF ("From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No." <> '') AND
                  NOT ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]) AND
                  ("From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type" = "From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type"::"Manufacturer Option")
               THEN BEGIN
                 VehOptionInvG.RESET;
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document Type","From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document No.","From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE(Type,"From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("No.","From Veh. Option Inv. No.");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Internal Code","From Veh. Opt.Inv. IntCode");
                 IF VehOptionInvG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
               // Start PA032776
                   OptionVariantG.RESET;
               // Stop PA032776
               // Start EU.0169755.165049
                   OptionVariantG.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.","Document Line No.","Document Type",Area);
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document No.", VehOptionInvG."Document No.");
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", VehOptionInvG."Document Line No.");
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Type", VehOptionInvG."Document Type");
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Area,OptionVariantG.Area::Sale);
               // Stop EU.0169755.165049
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Option Code", VehOptionInvG."Option Code");
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Internal Code", VehOptionInvG."Internal Code");
                   IF OptionVariantG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                     GetSalesHeader();
                     VarSaleHdrG.GET("From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type","From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.");
                     IF (SalesHeader."Currency Code" = VarSaleHdrG."Currency Code") OR (SalesHeader."Currency Code" = '') THEN BEGIN
                       IF SalesHeader."Currency Code" <> '' THEN
                         OptionVariantG.VALIDATE("Unit Price", "Unit Price")
                       ELSE
                         OptionVariantG.VALIDATE("Unit Price (LCY)", "Unit Price");
                     END ELSE BEGIN
                       GetSalesHeader();
                       CLEAR(Currency);
                       Currency.InitRoundingPrecision;  //Reset rounding of local currency
                       OptionVariantG.VALIDATE("Unit Price (LCY)",
                         ROUND(CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(SalesHeader."Posting Date",
                         SalesHeader."Currency Code","Unit Price",
               // Start PA040295
                         SalesHeader."Currency Factor"),Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision"));
               // Stop PA040295
                     END;
                     OptionVariantG.MODIFY;
                     VehOptionInvG."Unit Price" := OptionVariantG."Unit Price";
                     VehOptionInvG.Amount := OptionVariantG.Amount;
                     VehOptionInvG."Amount Including VAT" := OptionVariantG."Amount Including VAT";
                     VehOptionInvG."Available in Separate Invoice" := FALSE;
                     VehOptionInvG.MODIFY;
                     VarSaleLineG.GET("From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type","From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.","From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line");
                     VarSaleLineG.GetOptionPrice();
                     VarSaleLineG.MODIFY;
                   END;
                 END;
               END;
               IF ("From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No." <> '') AND
                  NOT ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]) AND
                  ("From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type" IN ["From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type"::"Own Option",
                  "From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type"::"Veh. Transfer","From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type"::Item,
                  "From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type"::"G/L Account"])
               THEN BEGIN
                 VehOptionInvG.RESET;
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document Type","From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document No.","From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE(Type,"From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type");
                 VehOptionInvG.SETRANGE("No.","From Veh. Option Inv. No.");
                 IF VehOptionInvG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                   IF VehOrderHdrL.GET("From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type","From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.") THEN BEGIN
                     IF VehOrderLineL.GET("From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type","From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.",
                        "From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line")
                     THEN
                       LineExistsL := TRUE
               // Start PA032178
                     ELSE BEGIN
                       LineExistsL := FALSE;
                       VehOrderLineL.INIT;
                       VehOrderLineL."Document Type" := "From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type";
                       VehOrderLineL."Document No." := "From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.";
                       VehOrderLineL."Line No." := "From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line";
                     END;
                     VehOrderLineL.TRANSFERFIELDS(Rec,FALSE);
               // Stop PA032178
                     VehOrderLineL."Sell-to Customer No." := VehOrderHdrL."Sell-to Customer No.";
                     VehOrderLineL."Attached to Line No." := 0;
                     VehOrderLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type" := 0;
                     VehOrderLineL."From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No." := '';
                     VehOrderLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line" := 0;
                     VehOrderLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type" := 0;
                     VehOrderLineL."From Veh. Option Inv. No." := '';
                     VehOrderLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. IntCode" := '';
                     IF LineExistsL THEN BEGIN
                       VehOrderLineL.MODIFY;
                     END ELSE BEGIN
               // Start PA032441
                       IF NOT VehOrderLineL.INSERT THEN BEGIN
               // Stop PA032441
                         VehOrderLineL.RESET;
                         VehOrderLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type");
                         VehOrderLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.");
                         IF VehOrderLineL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
               // Start PA032178
                           NextLineNoL := VehOrderLineL."Line No." + 10000;
                           VehOrderLineL.INIT;
                           VehOrderLineL."Document Type" := "From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type";
                           VehOrderLineL."Document No." := "From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.";
                           VehOrderLineL."Line No." := NextLineNoL;
                           VehOrderLineL.TRANSFERFIELDS(Rec,FALSE);
               // Stop PA032178
                           VehOrderLineL."Sell-to Customer No." := VehOrderHdrL."Sell-to Customer No.";
                           VehOrderLineL."Attached to Line No." := 0;
                           VehOrderLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type" := 0;
                           VehOrderLineL."From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No." := '';
                           VehOrderLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line" := 0;
                           VehOrderLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type" := 0;
                           VehOrderLineL."From Veh. Option Inv. No." := '';
                           VehOrderLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. IntCode" := '';
                           VehOrderLineL.INSERT;
                         END;
                       END;
                     END;
                   END;
                   VehOptionInvG."Unit Price" := "Unit Price";
                   VehOptionInvG.Amount := Amount;
                   VehOptionInvG."Amount Including VAT" := "Amount Including VAT";
                   VehOptionInvG.MODIFY;
               // Stop INC
                 END;
               END;

               IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Blanket Order" THEN BEGIN
                 SalesLine2.RESET;
                 SalesLine2.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Blanket Order No.","Blanket Order Line No.");
                 SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Blanket Order No.","Document No.");
                 SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Blanket Order Line No.","Line No.");
                 IF SalesLine2.FINDFIRST THEN
                   SalesLine2.TESTFIELD("Blanket Order Line No.",0);
               END;

               // Start INC
               // Start EU.0195242
               IF GUIALLOWED AND NOT DeleteQuietFlagG AND
                  ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Order,"Document Type"::Invoice]) AND
                  ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases")
               THEN
                 IF ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer") AND (VIN <> '') AND ("No." <> '') THEN BEGIN
                   VehLedgEntryL.RESET;
               // Start EU.0169755.165049
                   VehLedgEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Book No.",VIN);
                   VehLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Book No.","Book No.");
                   VehLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);
               // Stop EU.0169755.165049
                   VehLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Branch Book No.","Branch Book No.");
                   VehLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehLedgEntryL."Line Type"::"Veh. Transfer");
                   VehLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
                   VehLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(Open,TRUE);
                   VehLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(Positive,TRUE);
                   IF NOT VehLedgEntryL.ISEMPTY THEN
               // Start PA037205
                     IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC093,FALSE,"Item Type") THEN
                       ERROR('');
               // Stop PA037205
               END;
               // Stop EU.0195242
               IF Type = Type::Item THEN
                 DeleteItemChargeAssgnt("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
               IF Type = Type::"Charge (Item)" THEN
                 DeleteChargeChargeAssgnt("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
               // Start EU.0195242
               TransferExtendedTextG.DeleteSalesLines(Rec);
               // Stop EU.0195242
               // Start PA044975
               // Start EU.0010595.12463
               DeleteRelatedLines(NOT DeleteQuietFlagG);
               // Stop EU.0010595.12463
               // Stop PA044975
               OnDeleteDeleteSubTables();
               IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
                 ClearVehicleSetReference;

                       ERROR(C_INC081,VehicleOwnOptL."Service Order No.");
                     IF (VehicleOwnOptL."Service Order No." = '') AND (VehicleOwnOptL."Option Line No." = 0) THEN BEGIN
                       VehicleOwnOptL.DELETE(TRUE);
                     END ELSE BEGIN

                     END;
                   END;
                 END;
               END;

               TempVehDispPurchG.UpdateLinesFromSalesLine(Rec,TRUE);
               // Stop PA038126
               IF ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Quote,"Document Type"::Order,"Document Type"::Invoice]) AND
                  ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND
                  ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle)
               THEN BEGIN
                 SalesLineL.RESET;
                 SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
                 SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
                 SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Item Type","Item Type"::"Own Option");
                 SalesLineL.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);

                           VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Order Line No." := 0;
                           VehicleOwnOptL.MODIFY(TRUE);
                         END;
                       END;
                     END;
                   UNTIL SalesLineL.NEXT = 0;
                 END;
               END;

               // Start EU.0195242
               // Stop EU.0195242
               // Start EU.0098776

               SalesLineTempL.Quantity := "Outstanding Quantity";

               // Stop PA040667

               IF NOT SkipFindStatusG THEN
                 FindStatus(TRUE);
               // Stop EU.0090167
               // Stop EU.0095631
               // Start PA042968
               // Start EU.0104306
               IF Quantity <> "Quantity Invoiced" THEN
                 UpdateVATAmountRounding(TRUE);
                 // Stop EU.0104306
               // Stop PA042968

               // Stop PA041687

               // Stop EU.0020651

    { 15  ;   ;Quantity            ;Decimal       ;OnValidate=VAR

                                                                    Text002,

                                                                     ("Order Type" <> "Order Type"::Service) AND
                                                                     (Quantity - "Quantity Shipped" > 0)
                                                                  THEN

                                                                          ItemL.SETRANGE("Date Filter",0D,"Shipment Date");

                                                                          ItemBinL.SETRANGE("Location Code", "Location Code");
                                                                // Start PA036118
                                                                          IF NOT ItemBinL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                                                            ItemBinL."Item No." := "No.";
                                                                            ItemBinL."Location Code" := "Location Code";
                                                                // Start PA041776.70856
                                                                            ItemBinL."Bin Code" := "Bin Code";
                                                                // Stop PA041776.70856
                                                                          END;
                                                                // Stop PA036118
                                                                // Stop PA033019

                                                                // Start PA033343
                                                                // Start PA033343

                                                                             UserSessionUnitG.GetItemBinSet()
                                                                // Stop PA041776.70856

                                                                            UserSessionUnitG.GetItemBin(ItemBinL);

                                                                // Stop EU.0104306

                                                                  THEN

                                                                     ((ABS("Quantity (Base)") < ABS("Return Qty. Received (Base)")) AND ("Return Receipt No." = ''))
                                                                  THEN
                                                                    FIELDERROR("Quantity (Base)",STRSUBSTNO(Text003,FIELDCAPTION("Return Qty. Received (Base)")));

                                                                     ((ABS(Quantity) < ABS("Quantity Shipped")) AND ("Shipment No." = ''))
                                                                  THEN
                                                                    FIELDERROR(Quantity,STRSUBSTNO(Text003,FIELDCAPTION("Quantity Shipped")));
                                                                  IF ("Quantity (Base)" * "Qty. Shipped (Base)" < 0) OR

                                                                  THEN

                                                                END;
                                                                IF (Type = Type::"Charge (Item)") AND (CurrFieldNo <> 0) THEN BEGIN

                                                                    FIELDERROR(Quantity,STRSUBSTNO(Text003,FIELDCAPTION("Qty. Assigned")));
                                                                  UpdateItemChargeAssgnt;
                                                                END;

                                                                // Start PA033011.5954131

                                                                // Start PA040070.63485

                                                                // Stop INC

    { 18  ;   ;Qty. to Ship        ;Decimal       ;OnValidate=VAR
                                                                SalesLineL@1109400001 : Record 37;
                                                                ItemBinL@1109400002 : Record 5028749;
                                                                UserLocationL@1109400003 : Record 5028664;
                                                                ResQtyOnStockL@36900 : Decimal;
                                                                FirstReservationDateL@1737400 : Date;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036842
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036842
                                                                IF (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Qty. to Ship")) AND ("Service Order No." <> '') THEN
                                                                  ERROR(C_INC064,FIELDCAPTION("Qty. to Ship"),"Service Order No.");
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                // Start PA033986
                                                                // Start EU.0045397.45399
                                                                IF (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Qty. to Ship")) AND ("Additional Item" <> "Additional Item"::" ") THEN
                                                                  IF NOT AdditionalItemQtyConfirmation() THEN
                                                                    ERROR('');
                                                                // Stop EU.0045397.45399
                                                                // Stop PA033986
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                                // Start EU.0000369
                                                                ReservSetup.GET;
                                                                IF ReservSetup."Update Qty. to Ship" AND ("Reserved Quantity" <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                                                  ResQtyOnStockL := CalculateReserveQtyOnStock(FirstReservationDateL);
                                                                // Start EU.0032451
                                                                  IF Quantity <> "Quantity (Base)" THEN
                                                                    ResQtyOnStockL := ROUND(ResQtyOnStockL / "Qty. per Unit of Measure", 0.00001);;
                                                                // Stop EU.0032451
                                                                  IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Qty. to Ship") THEN BEGIN
                                                                    IF ResQtyOnStockL < "Qty. to Ship" THEN BEGIN
                                                                      IF ResQtyOnStockL = 0 THEN
                                                                        ERROR(C_INC_ResItemNotOnInventory, "No.")
                                                                      ELSE
                                                                        "Qty. to Ship" := ResQtyOnStockL;
                                                                    END;
                                                                // Start EU.0017374
                                                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                    IF NOT SuspendUpdateQtyToShipG THEN
                                                                      "Qty. to Ship" := ResQtyOnStockL;
                                                                  END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0017374
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0000369
                                                                IF "Qty. to Ship" = "Outstanding Quantity" THEN
                                                                  InitQtyToShip

                                                                  InitQtyToInvoice;
                                                                END;

                                                                   (ABS("Qty. to Ship") > ABS("Outstanding Quantity")) OR
                                                                   (Quantity * "Outstanding Quantity" < 0)
                                                                THEN
                                                                  ERROR(
                                                                    Text007,
                                                                    "Outstanding Quantity");
                                                                IF ("Qty. to Ship (Base)" * "Quantity (Base)" < 0) OR
                                                                   (ABS("Qty. to Ship (Base)") > ABS("Outstanding Qty. (Base)")) OR
                                                                   ("Quantity (Base)" * "Outstanding Qty. (Base)" < 0)
                                                                THEN
                                                                  ERROR(
                                                                    Text008,
                                                                    "Outstanding Qty. (Base)");

                                                                IF (CurrFieldNo <> 0) AND
                                                                   ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Order,"Document Type"::Invoice]) AND
                                                                   (Type = Type::Item) AND ("No." <> '') AND
                                                                   ("Item Type" <> "Item Type"::"Own Option") AND
                                                                   ("Qty. to Ship" > 0) AND ("Outstanding Quantity" > 0)
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                THEN BEGIN
                                                                  UserSessionUnitG.SetSalesLine(SalesLineL);
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                                  VehicleToDeliverCheckG.SalesLineCheck(Rec);

                                                                // Start EU.0128664.129600

                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                                  CASE "VAT Calculation Type" OF
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - SalesHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                        "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" / 100,Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                      END;
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                // Start EU.0145355.145511
                                                                        UnitCostL := "Unit Cost";
                                                                        IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
                                                                          UnitCostL := VehicleUnitG.CalculateVehicleUnitCostNoAdjust(VIN,"Book No.");
                                                                        IF Amount <= (Quantity * UnitCostL) THEN
                                                                          "VAT Base Amount" := 0
                                                                        ELSE
                                                                          "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND((Amount - (Quantity * UnitCostL)) *
                                                                // Stop EU.0145355.145511
                                                                            (1 - SalesHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                        "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" / 100, Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                        "Unit Price" := ROUND(Amount / Quantity, Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                // Start EU.0161230.157977
                                                                        IF GUIALLOWED AND ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND ("Unit Price" <> xRec."Unit Price") AND (xRec."Unit Price" <> 0) AND (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Amount)) THEN
                                                                          MESSAGE(C_INC094, "VAT Calculation Type", FIELDCAPTION("Unit Price"), xRec."Unit Price", "Unit Price");
                                                                // Stop EU.0161230.157977
                                                                // Stop INC

                                                                // Stop PA036994

                                                                          "Exch. Parts Tax Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                      END;

                                                                      IF Amount <> 0 THEN
                                                                        FIELDERROR(Amount,
                                                                          STRSUBSTNO(
                                                                            Text009,FIELDCAPTION("VAT Calculation Type"),
                                                                            "VAT Calculation Type"));
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        SalesHeader.TESTFIELD("VAT Base Discount %",0);

                                                                            "VAT Base Amount",Quantity,SalesHeader."Currency Factor");
                                                                // Stop EU.0104321
                                                                        IF "VAT Base Amount" <> 0 THEN
                                                                          "VAT %" :=
                                                                // Start PA036994

                                                                // Stop PA036994
                                                                        ELSE BEGIN
                                                                          "VAT %" := 0;
                                                                        END;
                                                                // Start EU.0104321
                                                                        "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND("Amount Including VAT", Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                // Stop EU.0104321
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                                      END;
                                                                  END;

                                                                THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF CONFIRM(C_INC089) THEN
                                                                    ResetFixedPrice
                                                                  ELSE
                                                                    ERROR('');

                                                                  UpdateItemChargeAssgnt();

                                                                    TESTFIELD("Unit Price");
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                                IF (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT")) AND ("Line No." = 0) AND ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) THEN
                                                                  ERROR(C_INC063);
                                                                // Start EU.0200720.199667
                                                                IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT") THEN
                                                                  IF "Amount Including VAT" <> xRec."Amount Including VAT" THEN
                                                                    UserSalesPriceChangePermG.SalesLinePriceChangeBlocked(Rec, FALSE);
                                                                // Stop EU.0200720.199667
                                                                // Start EU.0104306
                                                                TransactionStartedHereL := SetProcessTriggeredFromField(FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT"));
                                                                // Stop EU.0104306

                                                                GetSalesHeader;
                                                                "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND("Amount Including VAT",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");

                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                IF NOT ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Condition 1",FIELDNAME("Amount Including VAT")) THEN
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                                  CASE "VAT Calculation Type" OF
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                // Start EU.0055976
                                                                        UnitCostL := "Unit Cost";
                                                                        IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
                                                                          UnitCostL := VehicleUnitG.CalculateVehicleUnitCostNoAdjust(VIN,"Book No.");
                                                                // Stop EU.0055976
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" :=
                                                                          ROUND(
                                                                // Start EU.0055976
                                                                            ("Amount Including VAT" - (Quantity * UnitCostL)) /
                                                                // Stop EU.0055976
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                            (1 + (1 - SalesHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100) * "VAT %" / 100) , Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                                        IF "VAT Base Amount" < 0 THEN BEGIN
                                                                          "VAT Base Amount" := 0;
                                                                          Amount := "Amount Including VAT";
                                                                        END ELSE
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                // Start EU.0055976
                                                                          Amount := ROUND("VAT Base Amount" + (Quantity * UnitCostL), Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                // Stop EU.0055976
                                                                // Start PA036994
                                                                // Start PA040295
                                                                        "Unit Price" := ROUND(Amount / Quantity,Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                // Stop PA040295
                                                                // Stop PA036994
                                                                // Start EU.0161230.157977
                                                                        IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
                                                                          CorrectItemVariantPrice();
                                                                          IF GUIALLOWED AND ("Unit Price" <> xRec."Unit Price") AND (xRec."Unit Price" <> 0) AND (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT")) THEN
                                                                            MESSAGE(C_INC094, "VAT Calculation Type", FIELDCAPTION("Unit Price"), xRec."Unit Price", "Unit Price");
                                                                        END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0161230.157977
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                                      END;
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        Amount :=
                                                                          ROUND(
                                                                            ("Amount Including VAT" - "Exch. Parts Tax Amount") /
                                                                            (1 + (1 - SalesHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100) * "VAT %" / 100),Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - SalesHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                      END;
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        Amount :=
                                                                          ROUND(
                                                                            "Amount Including VAT" /
                                                                            (1 + (1 - SalesHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100) * "VAT %" / 100),Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - SalesHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                      END;
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        Amount := 0;
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := 0;
                                                                      END;
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        SalesHeader.TESTFIELD("VAT Base Discount %",0);
                                                                        Amount :=
                                                                // Start EU.0104321
                                                                          SalesTaxCalculate.ReverseCalculateTax(
                                                                            "Tax Area Code","Tax Group Code","Tax Liable",SalesHeader."Posting Date",
                                                                            "Amount Including VAT",Quantity,SalesHeader."Currency Factor");
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := Amount;
                                                                // Stop EU.0104321
                                                                        IF "VAT Base Amount" <> 0 THEN
                                                                          "VAT %" :=
                                                                            ROUND(100 * ("Amount Including VAT" - "VAT Base Amount") / "VAT Base Amount",0.00001)
                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                        ELSE BEGIN
                                                                          "VAT %" := 0;
                                                                        END;
                                                                // Start EU.0104321
                                                                        Amount := ROUND(Amount, Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := Amount;
                                                                // Stop EU.0104321
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                                      END;
                                                                  END;
                                                                // Stop PA034053.I000514

                                                                // Start INC
                                                                IF (CurrFieldNo <> 0) AND ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND Promotion AND
                                                                   ("Promotion Price incl. VAT" <> "Amount Including VAT")
                                                                THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF CONFIRM(C_INC089) THEN
                                                                    ResetFixedPrice
                                                                  ELSE
                                                                    ERROR('');
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                                // Start EU.0104306
                                                                InitManualVAT;
                                                                CalcLineInvDiscountFromAmount();
                                                                // Stop EU.0104306
                                                                InitOutstandingAmount();
                                                                CheckDiscount();

                                                                // Start EU.0137599.138014
                                                                IF NOT CalledFromCocpitOptionsG THEN
                                                                  DiscountOnOptionTable();
                                                                // Stop EU.0137599.138014
                                                                // Set change flag in OrderItemPriceCalculation
                                                                GetSalesHeader();
                                                                SalesLinePriceCalcG.SalesPriceCalcChange(Rec,SalesHeader);
                                                                // Start EU.0104306
                                                                RunOrderLineRounding(TransactionStartedHereL, xRec);
                                                                // Stop EU.0104306

                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,FIELDNAME("Amount Including VAT"));
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Amount Including VAT;
                                                   BlankZero=Yes;
                                                   Description=PA040837;
                                                   AutoFormatType=1;
                                                   AutoFormatExpr="Currency Code" }
    { 32  ;   ;Allow Invoice Disc. ;Boolean       ;InitValue=Yes;

    { 75  ;   ;Gen. Prod. Posting Group;Code10    ;TableRelation="Gen. Product Posting Group";
                                                   OnValidate=VAR
                                                                VatPostingSetupL@1109400000 : Record 325;
                                                                _INCADEA_@1109400002 : Boolean;
                                                                ItemL@1109400001 : Record 27;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036842
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036842
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                CheckOwnOptionPostingGroups();
                                                                IF (xRec."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" <> "Gen. Prod. Posting Group") AND
                                                                   (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Gen. Prod. Posting Group"))
                                                                THEN
                                                                  IF GenProdPostingGrp.ValidateVatProdPostingGroup(GenProdPostingGrp,"Gen. Prod. Posting Group") THEN
                                                                    IF VatPostingSetupL.GET("VAT Bus. Posting Group",GenProdPostingGrp."Def. VAT Prod. Posting Group") THEN BEGIN
                                                                      IF VatPostingSetupL."VAT Calculation Type" = VatPostingSetupL."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN  BEGIN
                                                                        IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
                                                                          VALIDATE("VAT Prod. Posting Group",GenProdPostingGrp."Def. VAT Prod. Posting Group");
                                                                      END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                        VALIDATE("VAT Prod. Posting Group",GenProdPostingGrp."Def. VAT Prod. Posting Group");
                                                                      END;
                                                                    END ELSE
                                                                IF ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Own Option" ) AND
                                                                   (ItemL.GET("No.") AND (ItemL."Accept posting group from Veh.")) AND
                                                                   (VehicleG.GET(VIN)) AND
                                                                   (VatPostingSetupL.GET("VAT Bus. Posting Group",VehicleG."VAT Prod. Posting Group")) AND
                                                                   (VatPostingSetupL."VAT Calculation Type" = VatPostingSetupL."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax")
                                                                THEN
                                                                  VALIDATE("VAT Prod. Posting Group",ItemL."VAT Prod. Posting Group")
                                                                ELSE
                                                                  VALIDATE("VAT Prod. Posting Group",GenProdPostingGrp."Def. VAT Prod. Posting Group");
                                                                CheckTaxFromPurchase;
                                                                IF ("VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax") AND
                                                                   ("Line Discount %" <> 0)
                                                                THEN
                                                                  ERROR(C_INC074,FIELDCAPTION("Line Discount %"),FIELDCAPTION("Gen. Prod. Posting Group"),"Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
                                                                UpdateServiceOrder(FIELDNO("Gen. Prod. Posting Group"));
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Gen. Prod. Posting Group }
    { 77  ;   ;VAT Calculation Type;Option        ;OnValidate=BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036842
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036842
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN BEGIN
                                                                  GetSalesHeader;
                                                                  IF SalesHeader."Payment Discount %" <> 0 THEN

                                                                IF "VAT Calculation Type" <> xRec."VAT Calculation Type" THEN
                                                                  DiscountOnOptionTable;

                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,FIELDNAME("VAT Prod. Posting Group"));

                                                              END;

    { 5407;   ;Unit of Measure Code;Code10        ;TableRelation=IF (Type=CONST(Item)) "Item Unit of Measure".Code WHERE (Item No.=FIELD(No.))
                                                                 ELSE "Unit of Measure";
                                                   OnValidate=VAR
                                                                UnitOfMeasureTranslation@1109400000 : Record 5402;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036842
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036842
                                                                IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Unit of Measure Code") THEN
                                                                  IF ("Additional Item" <> "Additional Item"::" ") AND ("Quantity Multiplier" <> 0) THEN
                                                                    ERROR(C_INC002,FIELDCAPTION("Unit of Measure Code"));
                                                                TESTFIELD("Quantity Shipped",0);
                                                                TESTFIELD("Qty. Shipped (Base)",0);
                                                                IF "Purch. Order Line No." <> 0 THEN
                                                                  ERROR(
                                                                    Text002,
                                                                    FIELDCAPTION("Unit of Measure Code"),"Purchase Order No.");
                                                                IF "Unit of Measure Code" = '' THEN
                                                                  "Unit of Measure" := ''
                                                                ELSE BEGIN
                                                                  IF NOT UnitOfMeasure.GET("Unit of Measure Code") THEN
                                                                    UnitOfMeasure.INIT;
                                                                  "Unit of Measure" := UnitOfMeasure.Description;
                                                                  GetSalesHeader;
                                                                  IF SalesHeader."Language Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                                                    UnitOfMeasureTranslation.SETRANGE(Code,"Unit of Measure Code");
                                                                    UnitOfMeasureTranslation.SETRANGE("Language Code",SalesHeader."Language Code");
                                                                    IF UnitOfMeasureTranslation.FINDFIRST THEN
                                                                      "Unit of Measure" := UnitOfMeasureTranslation.Description;
                                                                  END;
                                                                END;

                                                                        "Location Code" := VehicleG."Location Code";
                                                                // Start PA036118

                                                                          Description := VehicleG.Model;
                                                                      END ELSE BEGIN

                                                                        "Posting Group" := VehicleUnitG.FindInvPostGroup(Type = Type::Item, "No.", VIN, "Veh. Opt. Line No.",
                                                                          "Document Type", "Document No.");
                                                                        IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Own Option" THEN BEGIN

                                                                // Start PA032776

                                                                          VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group");

                                                                            THEN BEGIN

                                                                                "VAT Prod. Posting Group" := VehicleG."VAT Prod. Posting Group";
                                                                              END;

                                                                              "VAT Bus. Posting Group" := VehicleG."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)";

                                                                // Start PA032776

                                                                          END;
                                                                      END;

                                                                // Stop PA036002.26254

                                                                     (VehicleOptionG."Serial No." = '')

                                                                    VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Book No.",VehicleL."Current Book No.");

                                                                    VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Sales Order Line No.","Line No.");

                                                                IF IsImporter THEN BEGIN

                                                                    VehicleStocklistG.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
                                                                    VehicleStocklistG.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);

                                                                      ERROR(C_IMS004,VIN);
                                                                    COMMIT;

                                                                // Start PA036118
                                                                // Stop PA036118
                                                                // Stop PA035398.30661

                                                                  END ELSE

    { 5025407;;Date of Re-motorization;Date       ;OnValidate=VAR
                                                                VehicleL@1109400000 : Record 5025400;
                                                                UpdateL@1109400001 : Boolean;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA042167
                                                                TESTFIELD("Item Type","Item Type"::Vehicle);
                                                                IF ("Date of Re-motorization" <> 0D) AND ("Date of Re-motorization" < WORKDATE) THEN
                                                                  ERROR(C_INC_TooEarlyDate, FIELDCAPTION("Date of Re-motorization"),WORKDATE);
                                                                IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Order) AND ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") THEN
                                                                  IF (VIN <> '') AND VehicleL.GET(VIN) THEN BEGIN
                                                                    UpdateL := VehicleL."Date of Re-motorization" <> "Date of Re-motorization";
                                                                    IF UpdateL AND (xRec.VIN <> VIN) THEN
                                                                      UpdateL := "Date of Re-motorization" <> 0D;
                                                                    IF UpdateL THEN BEGIN
                                                                      VehicleL.VALIDATE("Date of Re-motorization","Date of Re-motorization");
                                                                      VehicleL.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                                                    END;
                                                                  END;
                                                                // Stop PA042167
                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Date of Re-motorization;
                                                   Description=PA042167 }
    { 5025420;No;FIELD ID 5025420 BLOCKED;Integer ;CaptionML=ENU=FIELD ID 5025420 BLOCKED;
                                                   Description=reserved for tables 37|111|113|115|6661|5028931|5046906 }

    { 5025438;;Print Option Line   ;Boolean       ;OnValidate=VAR

                                                                    ERROR(C_INC077, FIELDCAPTION("Print Option Line"), VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL.TABLECAPTION);
                                                                END;

                                                                IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
                                                                  "Print Option Line" := TRUE;
                                                                IF NOT "Print Option Line" THEN
                                                                  "Print Unit Price" := FALSE;
                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Print Option Line }

                                                                  ERROR(C_INC_Vehicle_Not_Exists);

                                                                  EXIT;

                                                                  IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC_Mileage_RunningTime,FALSE,FIELDCAPTION("Running Time")) THEN BEGIN
                                                                    "Running Time" := VehicleG."Running Time";

                                                                  END;

                                                                VehicleG.MODIFY(TRUE);

                                                              END;
