    { 5025841;;Supply VIN          ;Code20        ;TableRelation=Vehicle;
                                                   OnValidate=BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036842
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036842
                                                                // Start PA041023
                                                                IF (CurrFieldNo <> FIELDNO("Supply VIN")) AND ("Order Type" <> "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases") THEN
                                                                  TestIMSFieldAccess(CurrFieldNo);
                                                                // Stop PA041023
                                                                IF IsImporter THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF VehicleG.GET("Supply VIN") THEN BEGIN
                                                                    "Engine No." := VehicleG."Engine No.";
                                                                    "Transmission Type Code" := VehicleG."Transmission Type Code";
                                                                    "Key No." := VehicleG."Key No.";
                                                                    "Factory No." := VehicleG."Factory No.";
                                                                    DealerMgmtG.SalesLineFreightCheck(Rec);
                                                                  END;
                                                                  DealerMgmtG.UpdateResSalesLineReq(Rec);
                                                                END;
                                                                // Start PA041023
                                                                // Start PA041023.87192
                                                                IF ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases") AND (Type IN [Type::Item, Type::"Account (G/L)"]) THEN
                                                                // Stop PA041023.87192
                                                                  IF "Supply VIN" <> xRec."Supply VIN" THEN BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA041023.87058
                                                                    IF STRLEN("Supply VIN") > 17 THEN
                                                                      ERROR(C_INC_VINLengthError, TABLECAPTION, FIELDCAPTION("Supply VIN"));
                                                                // Stop PA041023.87058
                                                                // Start EU.0000497
                                                                    VehicleG.RESET;
                                                                    IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Supply VIN") THEN
                                                                      IF "Supply VIN" > '' THEN
                                                                        "Supply VIN" := VehicleG.VehicleSearch("Supply VIN");
                                                                // Stop EU.0000497
                                                                    IF VehicleG.GET("Supply VIN") THEN BEGIN
                                                                      VIN := "Supply VIN";
                                                                      "Reference License No." := VehicleG."License No.";
                                                                      "License No." := VehicleG."License No.";
                                                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                      VIN :=  '';
                                                                      "Reference License No." := '';
                                                                      "License No." := '';
                                                                    END;
                                                                    IF ("Serial No." <> '') AND ("Coded Part Type" <> '') THEN
                                                                      VehicleUnitG.UpdateCodedValue("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code", "No.", "Serial No.", "Supply VIN");
                                                                    IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Supply VIN") THEN
                                                                      UpdateReservedLinesFromSales();
                                                                  END;
                                                                // Stop PA041023
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                              END;

                                                   ValidateTableRelation=No;

                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036842
                                                                // Start PA032450
                                                                IF "Req. Worksheet Name" <> '' THEN
                                                                // Start PA032651
                                                                  IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Req. Worksheet Name") THEN BEGIN
                                                                    TESTFIELD("Order Type", "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases");
                                                                    TESTFIELD(Type, Type::Item);
                                                                  END;
                                                                IF (Type <> Type::Item) OR ("Order Type" <> "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases") THEN BEGIN
                                                                  "Req. Worksheet Name" := '';
                                                                END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                  GetSalesHeader();
                                                                  SalesHeader."Req. Wksh. Template Name" := ''; // <-- Currently its not in use. Field must be blank
                                                                  IF CurrFieldNo <> FIELDNO("Req. Worksheet Name") THEN BEGIN
                                                                    IF NOT ReqWorksheetFunctionsG.CheckReqWorksheetName(
                                                                      "Req. Worksheet Name",
                                                                      SalesHeader."Req. Wksh. Template Name",
                                                                      "Location Code",

                                                                      "No.",
                                                                      FALSE)
                                                                    THEN
                                                                      "Req. Worksheet Name" := '';
                                                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                    ReqWorksheetFunctionsG.SalesReqWorksheetNameChange(Rec, "Req. Worksheet Name", xRec."Req. Worksheet Name", TRUE);
                                                                    IF NOT ReqWorksheetFunctionsG.CheckReqWorksheetName(
                                                                      "Req. Worksheet Name",
                                                                      SalesHeader."Req. Wksh. Template Name",
                                                                      "Location Code",
                                                                      "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code",
                                                                      "No.",
                                                                      GUIALLOWED)
                                                                    THEN
                                                                      "Req. Worksheet Name" := xRec."Req. Worksheet Name";
                                                                  END;
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop PA032651
                                                                // Stop PA032450
                                                              END;

                                                   ValidateTableRelation=Yes;
                                                   TestTableRelation=No;
                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Req. Worksheet Name;
                                                   Description=PA032450 }

    PROCEDURE InitOutstanding@16();
    BEGIN
      IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN BEGIN
        "Outstanding Quantity" := Quantity - "Return Qty. Received";
        "Outstanding Qty. (Base)" := "Quantity (Base)" - "Return Qty. Received (Base)";
        "Return Qty. Rcd. Not Invd." := "Return Qty. Received" - "Quantity Invoiced";
        "Ret. Qty. Rcd. Not Invd.(Base)" := "Return Qty. Received (Base)" - "Qty. Invoiced (Base)";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        "Outstanding Quantity" := Quantity - "Quantity Shipped";
        "Outstanding Qty. (Base)" := "Quantity (Base)" - "Qty. Shipped (Base)";
        "Qty. Shipped Not Invoiced" := "Quantity Shipped" - "Quantity Invoiced";
        "Qty. Shipped Not Invd. (Base)" := "Qty. Shipped (Base)" - "Qty. Invoiced (Base)";
      END;
      Planned := "Reserved Quantity" = "Outstanding Quantity";
      InitOutstandingAmount;
      IF CurrFieldNo = 0 THEN
      // Start EU.0095631
        FindStatus(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0095631
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InitOutstandingAmount@17();
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'InitOutstandingAmount') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA036544

      IF Quantity = 0 THEN BEGIN
        "Outstanding Amount" := 0;
        "Outstanding Amount (LCY)" := 0;
        "Shipped Not Invoiced" := 0;
        "Shipped Not Invoiced (LCY)" := 0;
        "Return Rcd. Not Invd." := 0;
        "Return Rcd. Not Invd. (LCY)" := 0;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        GetSalesHeader;

      // Start PA036544
        ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 1",'InitOutstandingAmount');
      // Stop PA036544

        VALIDATE(
          "Outstanding Amount",
          ROUND(
            "Amount Including VAT" * "Outstanding Quantity" / Quantity,
            Currency."Amount Rounding Precision"));
        IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
          VALIDATE(
            "Return Rcd. Not Invd.",
            ROUND(
              "Amount Including VAT" * "Return Qty. Rcd. Not Invd." / Quantity,
              Currency."Amount Rounding Precision"))
        ELSE
          VALIDATE(
            "Shipped Not Invoiced",
            ROUND(
              "Amount Including VAT" * "Qty. Shipped Not Invoiced" / Quantity,
              Currency."Amount Rounding Precision"));
      END;

      // Start PA036544
      ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'InitOutstandingAmount');
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitQtyToShip@15();
    BEGIN
      "Qty. to Ship" := "Outstanding Quantity";
      "Qty. to Ship (Base)" := "Outstanding Qty. (Base)";
      InitQtyToInvoice;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitQtyToReceive@5803();
    BEGIN
      "Return Qty. to Receive" := "Outstanding Quantity";
      "Return Qty. to Receive (Base)" := "Outstanding Qty. (Base)";
      InitQtyToInvoice;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitQtyToInvoice@13();
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'InitQtyToInvoice') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA036544

      "Qty. to Invoice" := MaxQtyToInvoice;
      "Qty. to Invoice (Base)" := MaxQtyToInvoiceBase;

      // Start EU.0041404
      NoStatusChangeG := TRUE;
      // Stop EU.0041404
      IF CurrFieldNo = 0 THEN
      // Start EU.0095631
        FindStatus(FALSE);
      NoStatusChangeG := FALSE;
      // Stop EU.0095631

      // Start PA036544
      ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'InitQtyToInvoice');
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    PROCEDURE MaxQtyToInvoice@18() : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
        EXIT("Return Qty. Received" + "Return Qty. to Receive" - "Quantity Invoiced");
      // Stop INC
      EXIT("Quantity Shipped" + "Qty. to Ship" - "Quantity Invoiced");
    END;

    PROCEDURE MaxQtyToInvoiceBase@19() : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
        EXIT("Return Qty. Received (Base)" + "Return Qty. to Receive (Base)" - "Qty. Invoiced (Base)");

      EXIT("Qty. Shipped (Base)" + "Qty. to Ship (Base)" - "Qty. Invoiced (Base)");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalcBaseQty@14(Qty@1000 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("Qty. per Unit of Measure");
      EXIT(ROUND(Qty * "Qty. per Unit of Measure",0.00001));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SelectItemEntry@8(CurrentFieldNo@1000 : Integer);
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1109400001 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      // Start INC
      ItemLedgEntry.RESET;
      // Stop INC
      ItemLedgEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Variant Code",Open);
      ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
      // Start INC
      ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Correction,FALSE);
      IF "Location Code" <> '' THEN
        ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");

      CASE CurrentFieldNo OF
        FIELDNO("Appl.-to Item Entry"):
          BEGIN
            ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Positive,TRUE);
            ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Open,TRUE);
            IF ItemLedgEntry.GET("Appl.-to Item Entry") THEN
              ;
          END;
        FIELDNO("Appl.-from Item Entry"):
          BEGIN
            ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Positive,FALSE);
            IF ItemLedgEntry.GET("Appl.-from Item Entry") THEN
              ;
          END;
        FIELDNO("Serial No."):
      // Start PA034433
          BEGIN
      // Stop PA034433
            IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
              ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Positive,Quantity < 0)
            ELSE
              ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Positive,Quantity > 0);
      // Start PA034433
            IF Type = Type::Item THEN
              ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Open,TRUE);
          END;
      // Stop PA034433
      END;
      // Stop INC

      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Item Ledger Entries",ItemLedgEntry) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
      // Start INC
        CASE CurrentFieldNo OF
          FIELDNO("Appl.-to Item Entry"):
            "Appl.-to Item Entry" := ItemLedgEntry."Entry No.";
          FIELDNO("Appl.-from Item Entry"):
            "Appl.-from Item Entry" := ItemLedgEntry."Entry No.";
          FIELDNO("Serial No."):
            "Appl.-to Item Entry" := ItemLedgEntry."Entry No.";
        END;

      // Start EU.0055250
        GetSalesHeader();
        IF (("Shipment No." <> '') OR ("Return Receipt No." <> '')) OR
           ((SalesHeader."Applies-to Doc. No." <> '') AND
            (SalesHeader."Applies-to Doc. Type" <> SalesHeader."Applies-to Doc. Type"::" " ))
        THEN
          ItemLedgEntry.TESTFIELD("Location Code", "Location Code");
        IF ItemLedgEntry."Location Code" <> "Location Code" THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0055250
          "Location Code" := ItemLedgEntry."Location Code";
      // Start PA036118
      // Start EU.0055250
      // Stop EU.0055250
      // Start PA036549.34230
      // Start PA041187.87194
          LocationG.SalesCrossLocationCheck(FORMAT(Type), SalesHeader."Location Code", "Location Code", "Order Type", "Document Type");
      // Start PA041187.87194
      // Stop PA036549.34230
          LocationG.SalesCrossBranchCheck(SalesHeader, Rec);
      // Stop PA036118
      // Start EU.0055250
        END;
      // Stop EU.0055250
        "Serial No." := ItemLedgEntry."Serial No.";
        CheckSerialNo;
        "Book No." := ItemLedgEntry."Book No.";
        "Bin Code" := ItemLedgEntry."Bin Code";
        "Unit Cost (LCY)" := CalculateUnitCost(ItemLedgEntry);
        SalesLineL := Rec;
        CASE CurrentFieldNo OF
          FIELDNO("Appl.-to Item Entry"):
            SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Appl.-to Item Entry",ItemLedgEntry."Entry No.");
          FIELDNO("Appl.-from Item Entry"):
            SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Appl.-from Item Entry",ItemLedgEntry."Entry No.");
          FIELDNO("Serial No."):
            SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Serial No.",ItemLedgEntry."Serial No.");
        END;
      // Stop INC
        Rec := SalesLineL;
        IF Reserve <> Reserve::Always THEN
          CheckItemAvailable;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetSalesHeader@24(NewSalesHeader@1000 : Record 36);
    BEGIN
      SalesHeader := NewSalesHeader;

      // Start EU.0104306
      IF SalesHeader."Currency Code" = '' THEN BEGIN
        CLEAR(Currency);
        Currency.InitRoundingPrecision
      END ELSE BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0104306
        Currency.GET(SalesHeader."Currency Code");
        Currency.TESTFIELD("Amount Rounding Precision");
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetSalesHeader@1() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("Document No.");
      // Start PA034053.I000514
      IF ("Document Type" <> SalesHeader."Document Type") OR
         ("Document No." <> SalesHeader."No.") OR
         (SalesHeader."Location Code" = '')
      THEN BEGIN
        IF NOT SalesHeader.GET("Document Type","Document No.") THEN
          EXIT(FALSE);
      // Start EU.0104306
        SetSalesHeader(SalesHeader);
      END;
      // Stop EU.0104306

      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA034053.I000514
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetItem@9();
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      IF "No." <> Item."No." THEN
        Item.GET("No.");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateUnitPrice@2();
    VAR
      VehicleOptionL@1109400000 : Record 5025422;
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("Qty. per Unit of Measure");
      GetSalesHeader;
      PriceInCurrency := FALSE;
      ItemPriceInclVAT := FALSE;

      CASE Type OF
        Type::Item:
          BEGIN
            IF ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND (VIN <> '') AND VehicleG.GET(VIN) THEN BEGIN
              PriceInCurrency := TRUE;  //otherwise the current price in currency will be recalculated
            END ELSE BEGIN
              ItemPrice.INIT;
              ItemPrice."Item No." := "No.";
              ItemPrice."Price Group Code" := SalesHeader."Item Sales Price Group";
              ItemPrice."Currency Code" := SalesHeader."Currency Code";
              ItemPrice."Unit of Measure Code" := "Unit of Measure Code";
              IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Quote,"Document Type"::Order] THEN
      // Start INC
                ItemPrice."Starting Date" := WORKDATE
              ELSE
                ItemPrice."Starting Date" := SalesHeader."Posting Date";
              ItemPrice."Location Code" := "Location Code";
              ItemFindUnitPrice.RUN(ItemPrice);
      // Start PA034488
              "Unit Price" := ItemPrice."Unit Price";
      // Start PA034258.I001423
              IF IsImporter THEN
                IF (DealerMgmtG.GetDealer <> '') AND
      // Stop PA034258.I001423
                   ("Document Type" <> "Document Type"::"Credit Memo") AND
                   ("Unit Price" = 0) AND
                   NOT ("Item Type" IN ["Item Type"::"Own Option","Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer"]) AND
      // Start PA034521.I001387
                   NOT UserSessionG.GetBatchProcess
                THEN
      // Stop PA034521.I001387
                  ERROR(C_IMS009,"No.",FIELDCAPTION("Unit Price"));
      // Stop PA034488
              IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Own Option" THEN BEGIN
                IF Item.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA034252.I000372
                  IF VehicleOptionL.GET(VIN,"Veh. Opt. Line No.") AND
                     (Item."Select Unit Price" <> Item."Select Unit Price"::"Calc. Unit Price based on Profit%")
                  THEN BEGIN
                    "Unit Price" := ROUND(VehicleOptionL."Unit Price",Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
                  END ELSE BEGIN
      // Stop PA034252.I000372
                    CASE Item."Select Unit Price" OF
                      Item."Select Unit Price"::"Unit Price based on card":
                        BEGIN
                          "Unit Price" := Item."Unit Price";
                          "Unit Cost" := Item."Unit Cost";
                        END;
                      Item."Select Unit Price"::"Calc. Unit Price based on Profit%":
                        BEGIN
                          IF VehicleOptionL.GET(VIN,"Veh. Opt. Line No.") THEN BEGIN
                            IF Item."Profit %" < 100 THEN
      // Start PA040295
                              "Unit Price" := ROUND((VehicleOptionL."Unit Cost" / (1 - Item."Profit %" / 100)),Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
                            "Unit Cost" := ROUND(VehicleOptionL."Unit Cost",Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop PA040295
                          END ELSE BEGIN
                            "Unit Price" := 0;
                            "Unit Cost" := 0;
                          END;
                        END;
                    END;
      // Start PA034252.I000372
                  END;
      // Stop PA034252.I000372
                END;
              END;
      // Stop INC
              Item."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)" := ItemPrice."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)";
              "Allow Quantity Disc." := ItemPrice."Allow Quantity Disc.";
              IF "Order Type" <> "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
                "Allow Invoice Disc." := ItemPrice."Allow Invoice Disc.";
              "Allow Discount" := ItemPrice."Allow Discount";
      // Start INC
              IF IsImporter THEN
                Item.GET("No.");
      // Stop INC
              IF ItemPrice."Allow Cust./Item Disc." THEN BEGIN
                IF CustItemDisc.GET(SalesHeader."Cust./Item Disc. Gr.",Item."Cust./Item Disc. Gr.") THEN
                  "Cust./Item Disc. %" := CustItemDisc."Discount %";
              END ELSE
                "Cust./Item Disc. %" := 0;
              PriceInCurrency := ItemPrice."Currency Code" <> '';
              ItemPriceInclVAT := ItemPrice."Price Includes VAT";
      // Start PA044507
              IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer" THEN BEGIN
                IF VehicleUnitG.GetSalesDefaultTransFeeUnitPrice(Rec, FALSE, FALSE) THEN BEGIN
                  PriceInCurrency := FALSE;
                  ItemPriceInclVAT := FALSE;
                END;
              END;
      // Stop PA044507
            END;
          END;
        Type::Resource:
          BEGIN
            ResPrice.INIT;
      // Start PA031882
      // Stop PA031882
            ResPrice.Code := "No.";
            ResPrice."Work Type Code" := "Work Type Code";
            ResPrice."Currency Code" := "Currency Code";
            ResFindUnitPrice.RUN(ResPrice);
            "Unit Price" := ResPrice."Unit Price";
            PriceInCurrency := ResPrice."Currency Code" <> '';
          END;
      // Start INC
        Type::"Charge (Item)":
          UpdateItemChargeAssgnt;
      // Stop INC
      END;

      IF (SalesHeader."Currency Code" <> '') AND (NOT PriceInCurrency) THEN BEGIN
        SalesHeader.TESTFIELD("Currency Factor");
        "Unit Price" :=
          CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(
            GetDate,"Currency Code",
            "Unit Price",SalesHeader."Currency Factor");
      END;

      IF ItemPrice."Unit of Measure Code" = '' THEN
        "Unit Price" := "Unit Price" * "Qty. per Unit of Measure";

      IF ItemPriceInclVAT THEN BEGIN
        IF NOT VATPostingSetup.GET(Item."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)",Item."VAT Prod. Posting Group") THEN
          VATPostingSetup.INIT;
        CASE VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type" OF
          VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
            VATPostingSetup."VAT %" := 0;
          VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
      // Start INC
            ERROR(
              Text013,
              VATPostingSetup.FIELDCAPTION("VAT Calculation Type"),
              VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type");
      // Stop INC
          VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
            ERROR(C_INC016);
        END;
        CASE "VAT Calculation Type" OF
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
            "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT",
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
            BEGIN
              IF SalesHeader."Prices Including VAT" THEN BEGIN
                IF "VAT Bus. Posting Group" <> Item."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)" THEN
                  "Unit Price" := "Unit Price" * (100 + "VAT %") / (100 + VATPostingSetup."VAT %");
              END ELSE
                "Unit Price" := "Unit Price" / (1 + VATPostingSetup."VAT %" / 100);
            END;
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
            "Unit Price" := "Unit Price" / (1 + VATPostingSetup."VAT %" / 100);
        END;
      END ELSE
        IF SalesHeader."Prices Including VAT" THEN
          IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
            ERROR(C_INC017)
          ELSE
            "Unit Price" := "Unit Price" * (1 + "VAT %" / 100);
      Currency.TESTFIELD("Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
      "Unit Price" := ROUND("Unit Price",Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE FindResUnitCost@5();
    BEGIN
      ResCost.INIT;
      ResCost.Code := "No.";
      ResCost."Work Type Code" := "Work Type Code";
      ResFindUnitCost.RUN(ResCost);
      VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)",ResCost."Unit Cost");
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateAmounts@3();
    VAR
      UnitCostL@72000 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'UpdateAmounts') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA036544

      IF CurrFieldNo <> FIELDNO("Allow Invoice Disc.") THEN
        TESTFIELD(Type);
      GetSalesHeader;
      // Start PA042968
      // Start EU.0162969.163460
      OriginalAmount := CalcOriginalAmountUnrounded(Rec);
      // Stop EU.0162969.163460
      // Stop PA042968
      // Start PA034053.I000514

      // Start PA036544
      IF NOT ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Condition 1",'UpdateAmounts') THEN
      // Stop PA036544
        CASE "VAT Calculation Type" OF
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
            BEGIN
      // Start EU.0138596
              Amount := ROUND(OriginalAmount - "Line Discount Amount" + "Autom. Rounding Disc. Amount" - "Inv. Discount Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop EU.0138596
      // Start EU.0162969.163460
              IF "Line Discount %" = 100 THEN
                Amount := 0;
      // Stop EU.0162969.163460
              "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - SalesHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
              "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" / 100,Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
            END;
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
            BEGIN
      // Start EU.0055976
              UnitCostL := "Unit Cost";
              IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
                UnitCostL := VehicleUnitG.CalculateVehicleUnitCostNoAdjust(VIN,"Book No.");
      // Stop EU.0055976
      // Start INC
      // Start EU.0138596
              Amount := ROUND(OriginalAmount - "Line Discount Amount" + "Autom. Rounding Disc. Amount" - "Inv. Discount Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop EU.0138596
      // Start EU.0055976
              IF (Amount = 0) OR (Amount <= (Quantity * UnitCostL)) THEN
      // Stop EU.0055976
                "VAT Base Amount" := 0
              ELSE
      // Start EU.0055976
                "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND((Amount - (Quantity * UnitCostL)) *
      // Stop EU.0055976
                  (1 - SalesHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
              "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" / 100,Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop INC
            END;
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax":
            BEGIN
      // Start EU.0138596
              Amount := ROUND(OriginalAmount - "Line Discount Amount" + "Autom. Rounding Disc. Amount" - "Inv. Discount Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop EU.0138596
              "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - SalesHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Start PA036994
              "Exch. Parts Tax Base" := ROUND(OriginalAmount*"Exch. Parts Tax %" / 100,Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop PA036994
              "Exch. Parts Tax Amount" := ROUND("Exch. Parts Tax Base" * "Exch. Parts VAT %" / 100,Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
              "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" /100 +
                 "Exch. Parts Tax Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
            END;
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
            BEGIN
              Amount := 0;
              "VAT Base Amount" := 0;
              "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(OriginalAmount);
            END;
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
            BEGIN
      // Start EU.0138596
              Amount := ROUND(OriginalAmount - "Line Discount Amount" + "Autom. Rounding Disc. Amount" - "Inv. Discount Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop EU.0138596
              "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount,Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
              "Amount Including VAT" :=
      // Start EU.0104321
                Amount +
                  SalesTaxCalculate.CalculateTax(
                    "Tax Area Code","Tax Group Code","Tax Liable",SalesHeader."Posting Date",
                    "VAT Base Amount",Quantity,SalesHeader."Currency Factor");
      // Stop EU.0104321
              IF "VAT Base Amount" <> 0 THEN
                "VAT %" :=
                  ROUND(100 * ("Amount Including VAT" - "VAT Base Amount") / "VAT Base Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision")
             ELSE BEGIN
               "VAT %" := 0;
             END;
      // Start EU.0104321
             "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND("Amount Including VAT", Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop EU.0104321
          END;
        END;
      // Stop PA034053.I000514

      // Start INC
      IF (CurrFieldNo <> 0) AND ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND Promotion AND
         ("Promotion Price incl. VAT" <> "Amount Including VAT")
      THEN BEGIN
        IF CONFIRM(C_INC089) THEN
          ResetFixedPrice
        ELSE
          ERROR('');
      // Start EU.0104306
      END;
      // Stop INC
      InitManualVAT;
      // Stop EU.0104306

      InitOutstandingAmount;
      // Start INC
      IF Type = Type::"Charge (Item)" THEN
        UpdateItemChargeAssgnt();
      // Stop INC

      // Start PA036544
      ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'UpdateAmounts');
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    PROCEDURE SkipUpdateVATAmountRounding@1109400024();
    BEGIN
      // Start PA040295.57698
      SkipUpdateVATAmountRoundingG := TRUE;
      // Stop PA040295.57698
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SetProcessTriggeredFromField@10430615(FromFieldNoP@10430600 : Integer) TransactionStartDetected : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      IF ProcessTriggeredFromFieldG <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      ProcessTriggeredFromFieldG := FromFieldNoP;
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE RunOrderLineRounding@10430614(TransactionStartDetectedP@10430601 : Boolean;ExRecP@10430600 : Record 37);
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      IF TransactionStartDetectedP THEN BEGIN
        IF (ExRecP.Amount = 0) OR (ExRecP."Amount Including VAT" = 0) THEN
          IF NOT ExRecP.GET(RECORDID) THEN
            ;
        IF UpdateVATAmountRounding(FALSE) THEN
          IF (Amount <> ExRecP.Amount) OR ("Amount Including VAT" <> ExRecP."Amount Including VAT") THEN
            InitOutstandingAmount();
        ProcessTriggeredFromFieldG := 0;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateVATAmountRounding@1000000001(SkipCurrentLineP@1000000000 : Boolean) CurrLineAdjustedR : Boolean;
    VAR
      ExRecL@1000 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to detect cent rounding difference coming from the 2 decimals "VAT Amount" calculation of the "Amount" and the "Amount including VAT"
      // @ In case there are some the difference it added to the current "Amount including VAT"
      // Start EU.0104306
      IF SkipUpdateVATAmountRoundingG THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      IF ("Unit Price" = 0) OR ("VAT %" = 0) OR (Quantity = 0) THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      // Start EU.0145355.145511
      IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0145355.145511
      GetSalesHeader();
      IF SalesHeader."Prices Including VAT" THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      GeneralLedgerSetupG.GetRec();
      ExRecL := Rec;
      CASE "Order Type" OF
        "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
          IF GeneralLedgerSetupG."Parts Sales VAT Rounding Adj." = GeneralLedgerSetupG."Parts Sales VAT Rounding Adj."::"Directly when modify a Line" THEN
            UpdateLineVATAmountRounding(SkipCurrentLineP);
        "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
          IF GeneralLedgerSetupG."Veh. Sales VAT Rounding Adj." = GeneralLedgerSetupG."Veh. Sales VAT Rounding Adj."::"Directly when modify a Line" THEN
            UpdateLineVATAmountRounding(SkipCurrentLineP);
        "Order Type"::Service:
      // Start EU.0132795
          IF GeneralLedgerSetupG."Service VAT Rounding Adjustm." = GeneralLedgerSetupG."Service VAT Rounding Adjustm."::"Directly when modify a Line" THEN
      // Stop EU.0132795
            UpdateLineVATAmountRounding(SkipCurrentLineP);
      END;
      EXIT((Amount <> ExRecL.Amount) OR ("Amount Including VAT" <> ExRecL."Amount Including VAT") OR ("Line Discount %" <> ExRecL."Line Discount %"));
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    PROCEDURE CallVATAmountAdjustment@10430601(SalesHdrP@1109400002 : Record 36);
    VAR
      RecL@10430600 : Record 37;
      DummyRecL@10430604 : Record 37;
      TempStatisticsEnhancedKey@10430601 : TEMPORARY Record 5028980;
      VatKeyL@10430602 : Code[20];
      AdjustmentFieldIDL@10430603 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to run a full VAT Rounding Adjustment run over all Sales Lines.
      // @ Currently called from the Create Service Invoice Codeunit.
      // Start EU.0132795
      GeneralLedgerSetupG.GetRec();
      CASE SalesHdrP."Order Type" OF
        SalesHdrP."Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
          IF GeneralLedgerSetupG."Parts Sales VAT Rounding Adj." = GeneralLedgerSetupG."Parts Sales VAT Rounding Adj."::"No Pre-Posting Adjustment" THEN
            EXIT;
        SalesHdrP."Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
          IF GeneralLedgerSetupG."Veh. Sales VAT Rounding Adj." = GeneralLedgerSetupG."Veh. Sales VAT Rounding Adj."::"No Pre-Posting Adjustment" THEN
            EXIT;
        SalesHdrP."Order Type"::Service:
          IF GeneralLedgerSetupG."Service VAT Rounding Adjustm." = GeneralLedgerSetupG."Service VAT Rounding Adjustm."::"No Pre-Posting Adjustment" THEN
            EXIT;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0132795
      // Start EU.0104306
      "Document Type" := SalesHdrP."Document Type";
      "Document No." := SalesHdrP."No.";
      GetSalesHeader();
      RecL.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHdrP."Document Type");
      RecL.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHdrP."No.");
      RecL.SETFILTER(Type, '<>%1', Type::" ");
      RecL.SETFILTER(Quantity, '<>0');
      RecL.SETFILTER("VAT %", '<>0');
      RecL.SETFILTER("Unit Price", '<>0');
      // Start EU.0132795
      RecL.SETFILTER("Line Discount %", '<>100');
      // Stop EU.0132795
      IF NOT GeneralLedgerSetupG.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicInDocActive(SalesHdrP."VAT Calculation Logic") THEN BEGIN
        AdjustmentFieldIDL := FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT");
      END ELSE BEGIN
        AdjustmentFieldIDL := FIELDNO(Amount);
      END;
      IF RecL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          VatKeyL := STRSUBSTNO('%1/%2',RecL."VAT %", RecL."VAT Calculation Type" + 0);
          IF NOT TempStatisticsEnhancedKey.GET(0,0,VatKeyL,RecL."Bill-to Customer No.",'', 0) THEN BEGIN
            TempStatisticsEnhancedKey.INIT;
            TempStatisticsEnhancedKey.A := VatKeyL;
            TempStatisticsEnhancedKey.B := RecL."Bill-to Customer No.";
            TempStatisticsEnhancedKey.Int01 := RecL."Line No.";
            TempStatisticsEnhancedKey.INSERT;
          END;
        UNTIL RecL.NEXT = 0;
        TempStatisticsEnhancedKey.FINDSET;
        REPEAT
          RecL.GET(SalesHdrP."Document Type", SalesHdrP."No.", TempStatisticsEnhancedKey.Int01);
          RecL.SETRANGE("VAT %", RecL."VAT %");
          RecL.SETRANGE("Bill-to Customer No.", RecL."Bill-to Customer No.");
          RecL.SETRANGE("VAT Calculation Type", RecL."VAT Calculation Type");
      // Start EU.0139128.139350
          DummyRecL := RecL;
          AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT(DummyRecL, RecL, AdjustmentFieldIDL, TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0139128.139350
        UNTIL TempStatisticsEnhancedKey.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateLineVATAmountRounding@1109400040(SkipCurrentLineP@1000000000 : Boolean);
    VAR
      RecL@10430600 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to detect cent rounding difference coming from the 2 decimals "VAT Amount" calculation of the "Amount" and the "Amount including VAT"
      // @ In case there are some the difference it added to the current "Amount including VAT"
      // Add the unrounded "Amount Including VAT" for the other lines
      // Start EU.0104306
      RecL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      RecL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      RecL.SETFILTER(Type, '<>%1', Type::" ");
      RecL.SETFILTER(Quantity, '<>0');
      RecL.SETFILTER("Unit Price", '<>0');
      // Start EU.0132795
      RecL.SETFILTER("Line Discount %", '<>100');
      // Stop EU.0132795
      RecL.SETRANGE("VAT %","VAT %");
      RecL.SETRANGE("Bill-to Customer No.","Bill-to Customer No.");
      RecL.SETRANGE("VAT Calculation Type", "VAT Calculation Type");
      RecL.SETRANGE("VAT Identifier", "VAT Identifier");
      IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax" THEN BEGIN
        AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT(Rec, RecL, FIELDNO("Exch. Parts Tax Base"), SkipCurrentLineP);
        AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT(Rec, RecL, FIELDNO("Exch. Parts Tax Amount"), SkipCurrentLineP);
      END;
      IF NOT GeneralLedgerSetupG.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicInDocActive(SalesHeader."VAT Calculation Logic") THEN BEGIN
        AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT(Rec, RecL, FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT"), SkipCurrentLineP);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT(Rec, RecL, FIELDNO(Amount), SkipCurrentLineP);
      END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT@1000000004(VAR CurLineP@1000000006 : Record 37;VAR LineP@1000000005 : Record 37;AdjustmentFieldIDP@1000000004 : Integer;SkipCurrentLineP@1000000000 : Boolean);
    VAR
      LastLineL@13279500 : Record 37;
      ExLineL@10430600 : Record 37;
      CurrencyL@1001 : Record 4;
      TotalAmountUnroundedL@1109400001 : Decimal;
      TotalAmountL@1002 : Decimal;
      CurrLineProcessedL@10430601 : Boolean;
      UseTotalAmountsL@13279501 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to detect cent rounding difference coming from the 2 decimals "VAT Amount" calculation of the "Amount" and the "Amount including VAT"
      // @ In case there are some the difference it added to the current "Amount including VAT"
      // Start PA042968
      // Add the unrounded "Amount Including VAT" for the other lines
      // Start EU.0104306
      CurrencyL := Currency;
      IF AdjustmentFieldIDP = FIELDNO(Amount) THEN
        CASE Currency.VATRoundingDirection OF
          '>':
            CurrencyL."VAT Rounding Type" := CurrencyL."VAT Rounding Type"::Down;
          '<':
            CurrencyL."VAT Rounding Type" := CurrencyL."VAT Rounding Type"::Up;
        END;

      // Start EU.0132795
      IF LineP.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        UseTotalAmountsL :=
           (CurLineP."VAT Calculation Type" IN [CurLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT", CurLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT"]) AND
           (AdjustmentFieldIDP IN [FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT"), FIELDNO(Amount)]);
      // Stop EU.0132795
        REPEAT
          ExLineL := LineP;
          IF LineP."Line No." = CurLineP."Line No." THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0138596
            CurrLineProcessedL := TRUE;
      // Stop EU.0138596
            IF NOT SkipCurrentLineP THEN
      // Start EU.0132795
              AdjustVATRoundingRestOneLine(CurLineP, AdjustmentFieldIDP, CurrencyL, TotalAmountUnroundedL, TotalAmountL, UseTotalAmountsL);
          END ELSE BEGIN
            AdjustVATRoundingRestOneLine(LineP, AdjustmentFieldIDP, CurrencyL, TotalAmountUnroundedL, TotalAmountL, UseTotalAmountsL);
      // Stop EU.0132795
            IF (LineP.Amount <> ExLineL.Amount) OR
               (LineP."Amount Including VAT" <> ExLineL."Amount Including VAT") OR
               (LineP."Line Discount %" <> ExLineL."Line Discount %") OR
      // Start EU.0138596
               (LineP."Autom. Rounding Disc. %" <> ExLineL."Autom. Rounding Disc. %") OR
      // Stop EU.0138596
               (LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base" <> ExLineL."Exch. Parts Tax Base") OR
               (LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" <> ExLineL."Exch. Parts Tax Amount")
            THEN
              LineP.MODIFY;
          END;
      // Start EU.0138596
      // Stop EU.0138596
        UNTIL LineP.NEXT = 0;
        IF NOT CurrLineProcessedL THEN
          IF NOT SkipCurrentLineP THEN
      // Start EU.0132795
      // Start EU.0138596
            IF CurLineP."Line No." <> 0 THEN
      // Stop EU.0138596
            AdjustVATRoundingRestOneLine(CurLineP, AdjustmentFieldIDP, CurrencyL, TotalAmountUnroundedL, TotalAmountL, UseTotalAmountsL);
      END;
      // Stop EU.0132795
      // Stop EU.0104306
      // Stop PA042968
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE AdjustVATRoundingRestOneLine@10430600(VAR LineP@1000000005 : Record 37;AdjustmentFieldIDP@1000000004 : Integer;CurrencyP@10430600 : Record 4;VAR TotalAmountUnroundedP@10430602 : Decimal;VAR TotalAmountP@10430601 : Decimal;UseTotalAmountsP@13279501 : Boolean);
    VAR
      DummyLineL@13279502 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to detect cent rounding difference in one line
      // @ UseTotalAmountsP = indicator which controls if the rounding rest is calculated over summed up single line values or the sum on all lines.
      // @                    True = All lines are summed up and then the VAT is calculated to - or out of it.
      // @                    False = In each line the VAT is calculated to - or of the Amount and then the values are summed up to totals.
      // @                            This method must be used for all lines which are not "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT" or "Reverse Charge VAT".
      // @                    Each way sound identical but there can be a small rounding happen when we don't use the "True" way.
      // Start EU.0104306
      CASE AdjustmentFieldIDP OF
        FIELDNO("Exch. Parts Tax Base"):
          BEGIN
      // Start EU.0132795
            TotalAmountUnroundedP += CalcOriginalAmount(LineP) * LineP."Exch. Parts Tax %" / 100;
            LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base" := ROUND(TotalAmountUnroundedP, CurrencyP."Amount Rounding Precision", CurrencyP.VATRoundingDirection) - TotalAmountP;
            TotalAmountP += LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base";
      // Stop EU.0132795
          END;
        FIELDNO("Exch. Parts Tax Amount"):
          BEGIN
      // Start EU.0132795
            TotalAmountUnroundedP += LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base" * LineP."Exch. Parts VAT %" / 100;
            LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" := ROUND(TotalAmountUnroundedP, CurrencyP."Amount Rounding Precision", CurrencyP.VATRoundingDirection) - TotalAmountP;
            TotalAmountP += LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount";
      // Stop EU.0132795
          END;
        FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT"):
          BEGIN
      // Start EU.0132795
            IF UseTotalAmountsP THEN BEGIN
              TotalAmountUnroundedP += LineP.Amount;
              DummyLineL := LineP;
              DummyLineL.Amount := TotalAmountUnroundedP;
              DummyLineL."Amount Including VAT" := DummyLineL.CalcVATAmountUnrounded(DummyLineL);
            END ELSE BEGIN
              TotalAmountUnroundedP += CalcVATAmountUnrounded(LineP);
              DummyLineL."Amount Including VAT" := TotalAmountUnroundedP;
            END;
            LineP."Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(DummyLineL."Amount Including VAT", CurrencyP."Amount Rounding Precision", CurrencyP.VATRoundingDirection) - TotalAmountP;
            TotalAmountP += LineP."Amount Including VAT";
      // Stop EU.0132795
          END;
        FIELDNO(Amount):
          BEGIN
      // Start EU.0132795
            IF UseTotalAmountsP THEN BEGIN
              TotalAmountUnroundedP += LineP."Amount Including VAT";
              DummyLineL := LineP;
              DummyLineL."Amount Including VAT" := TotalAmountUnroundedP;
              DummyLineL.Amount := DummyLineL.CalcAmountUnrounded(DummyLineL);
            END ELSE BEGIN
              TotalAmountUnroundedP += CalcVATAmountUnrounded(LineP);
              DummyLineL.Amount := TotalAmountUnroundedP;
            END;
            LineP.Amount := ROUND(DummyLineL.Amount, CurrencyP."Amount Rounding Precision", CurrencyP.VATRoundingDirection) - TotalAmountP;
            TotalAmountP += LineP.Amount;
            GetSalesHeader();
            // Calc new Line Discount
            CalcLineDiscount(
              LineP.Amount,
              LineP."Line Discount Amount",
              LineP."Line Discount %",
      // Start EU.0138596
              LineP."Autom. Rounding Disc. Amount",
              LineP."Autom. Rounding Disc. %",
      // Stop EU.0138596
              CurrencyP."Amount Rounding Precision",
              CalcOriginalAmountUnrounded(LineP));
      // Stop EU.0132795
          END;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcLineDiscount@12971301(AmountP@1000000005 : Decimal;VAR LineDiscountAmountP@12971303 : Decimal;VAR LineDiscountP@12971302 : Decimal;VAR RoundingDiscountAmountP@1385961 : Decimal;VAR RoundingDiscountP@1385960 : Decimal;VAR AmountRoundingPrecisionP@12971300 : Decimal;OriginalAmountP@12971301 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      // @ Function to calculate the Line Discount % and the Discount Amount
      // Start EU.0132795
      OriginalAmountP := ROUND(OriginalAmountP, AmountRoundingPrecisionP);
      // Start EU.0138596
      IF OriginalAmountP = 0 THEN BEGIN
          LineDiscountP := 0;
        LineDiscountAmountP := 0;
        RoundingDiscountP := 0;
        RoundingDiscountAmountP := 0;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        LineDiscountP := LineDiscountP - RoundingDiscountP;
        RoundingDiscountAmountP := OriginalAmountP - AmountP - (LineDiscountAmountP - RoundingDiscountAmountP);
        IF OriginalAmountP <> 0 THEN
          RoundingDiscountP := ROUND(RoundingDiscountAmountP / OriginalAmountP * 100, 0.00001)
        ELSE
          RoundingDiscountP := 0;
        LineDiscountP := LineDiscountP + RoundingDiscountP;
        LineDiscountAmountP := ROUND(OriginalAmountP * LineDiscountP / 100, AmountRoundingPrecisionP);
      END;
      // Stop EU.0138596
      // Stop EU.0132795
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcVATAmountUnrounded@1109400021(VAR SalesLineP@1109400001 : Record 37) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to calculate "Amount including VAT" out of the Amount with high precision
      // Start PA040295
      CASE SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type" OF
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
      // Start PA040256.61743
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
          EXIT(SalesLineP.Amount + SalesLineP.Amount * SalesLineP."VAT %" / 100);
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
          EXIT(SalesLineP.Amount + SalesLineP."VAT Base Amount" * SalesLineP."VAT %" / 100);
      // Stop PA040256.61743
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax":
      // Start PA042968
          EXIT(SalesLineP.Amount + SalesLineP."VAT Base Amount" * SalesLineP."VAT %" / 100 + SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount");
      // Stop PA042968
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
      // Start PA040837
          BEGIN
            GetSalesHeader();
            EXIT(SalesLineP.Amount + SalesTaxCalculate.CalculateTax(
              SalesLineP."Tax Area Code",
              SalesLineP."Tax Group Code",
              SalesLineP."Tax Liable",
              SalesHeader."Posting Date",
              SalesLineP."VAT Base Amount",
              SalesLineP.Quantity,
              SalesHeader."Currency Factor"));
          END;
      // Stop PA040837
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
          EXIT(SalesLineP."Amount Including VAT");
      END;
      // Stop PA040295
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcAmountUnrounded@10329508(VAR RecP@1109400001 : Record 37) : Decimal;
    VAR
      RecL@1000 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to calculate the Amount out of the "Amount including VAT" with high precision
      // Start EU.0104306
      CASE RecP."VAT Calculation Type" OF
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
          EXIT(RecP."Amount Including VAT" / (1 + RecP."VAT %" / 100));
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
      // Start EU.0128664.129600
          BEGIN
            RecL := Rec;
            IF RecP."Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
              RecL."Unit Cost" := VehicleUnitG.CalculateVehicleUnitCostNoAdjust(RecP.VIN, RecP."Book No.");
            RecL."Amount Including VAT" -= RecL."Unit Cost";
            IF RecL."Amount Including VAT" > 0 THEN
              EXIT((RecL."Amount Including VAT" / (1 + RecL."VAT %" / 100)) + RecL."Unit Cost")
            ELSE
              EXIT(RecL."Amount Including VAT"  + RecL."Unit Cost");
          END;
      // Stop EU.0128664.129600
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax":
          EXIT((RecP."Amount Including VAT" - RecP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount") / (1 + (1 - SalesHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100) * RecP."VAT %" / 100));
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
          BEGIN
            GetSalesHeader();
            EXIT(SalesTaxCalculate.ReverseCalculateTax(
              RecP."Tax Area Code",
              RecP."Tax Group Code",
              RecP."Tax Liable",
              SalesHeader."Posting Date",
              RecP."Amount Including VAT",
              RecP.Quantity,
              SalesHeader."Currency Factor"));
          END;
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
          EXIT(0);
      END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcOriginalAmount@6(LineP@1000000000 : Record 37) : Decimal;
    VAR
      OriginalAmountL@1000000001 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      GetSalesHeader;
      // Start PA042968
      OriginalAmountL := CalcOriginalAmountUnrounded(LineP);
      EXIT(ROUND(OriginalAmountL, Currency."Amount Rounding Precision"));
      // Stop PA042968
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalcOriginalAmountUnrounded@1000000000(LineP@1000000000 : Record 37) OrigAmountR : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA042968
      OrigAmountR := LineP.Quantity * LineP."Unit Price";
      IF SalesHeader."Prices Including VAT" THEN
        CASE "VAT Calculation Type" OF
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT",
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
            OrigAmountR := LineP.Quantity * LineP."Unit Price" / (1 + LineP."VAT %" / 100);
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
            OrigAmountR := LineP.Quantity * LineP."Unit Price";
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
            ERROR(C_INC017);
        END ELSE
          OrigAmountR := LineP.Quantity * LineP."Unit Price";
      // Stop PA042968
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckItemAvailable@4();
    VAR
      VehicleAvailOnHand@1109400000 : Codeunit 5028660;
      _INCADEA_@1101353001 : Boolean;
      DealerCheckItemsToShipL@1101353000 : Codeunit 5086703;
    BEGIN
      // @ When creating sales lines using code, if this function is required to be executed, just set the ValidateAvailableQtyG
      // @ variable to TRUE by calling the SetValidateAvailableQty function. By default ValidateAvailableQtyG would be false
      // Start INC
      IF ((CurrFieldNo <> 0) OR ("Additional Item" = "Additional Item"::"Additional Item") OR ValidateAvailableQtyG) AND
         ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Order,"Document Type"::Invoice]) AND
         (Type = Type::Item) AND ("No." <> '') AND
         ("Outstanding Quantity" > 0) AND
      // Start PA031882
         ("Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle)
      // Stop PA031882
      THEN BEGIN
        IF IsImporter() THEN BEGIN
          IF (DealerMgmtG.GetDealer() <> '') AND
             DealerSetupG.GET(DealerMgmtG.GetDealer()) AND
             (NOT DealerSetupG."Disable Parts Backorder")
          THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA033019.9419648
            DealerCheckItemsToShipL.SetValidateQuantity(CurrFieldNo <> (FIELDNO(Quantity)));
            DealerCheckItemsToShipL.SalesLineCheck(Rec);
            DealerCheckItemsToShipL.SetValidateQuantity(TRUE);
      // Stop PA033019.9419648
      // Start PA034053.I000514
            GetSalesHeader();
      // Stop PA034053.I000514
          END ELSE
            VehicleAvailOnHand.CalculateSalesLine(Rec);
        END ELSE
          VehicleAvailOnHand.CalculateSalesLine(Rec);
      // Start PA032178
      // Start EU.0174523
        IF NOT ISTEMPORARY THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0174523
        SalesHeader.GET("Document Type", "Document No.");
      // Stop PA032178
        SalesHeader.UpdateStatus();
        SalesHeader.MODIFY;
      // Start EU.0174523
      END;
      // Stop EU.0174523
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE ShowReservation@10();
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      // Start EU.0000369
      ReservMgt.CheckAllowReserveForSales("Document Type", TRUE);
      IF Reserve = Reserve::Never THEN
        ERROR(C_INC_ErrCheckReservation, FIELDCAPTION(Reserve), Reserve);
      // Stop EU.0000369
      IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
        CLEAR(ReservVehG);
        ReservVehG.SetSalesLine(Rec);
        ReservVehG.RUNMODAL;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        CLEAR(Reservation);
        Reservation.SetSalesLine(Rec);
        Reservation.RUNMODAL;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ShowReservationEntries@21(Modal@1000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      IF Signed("Quantity (Base)") < 0 THEN BEGIN
        ReservMgt.InitFilterAndSortingLookupFor(ReservEntry,TRUE);
        ReservMgt.SalesLineFilterReservFor(ReservEntry,Rec);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        ReservMgt.InitFilterAndSortingLookupFrom(ReservEntry,TRUE);
        ReservMgt.SalesLineFilterReservFrom(ReservEntry,Rec);
      END;

      // Start INC
      ResPageG := PAGE::"Reservation Entries";
      IF IsImporter() THEN
        IF DealerMgmtG.GetDealer() <> '' THEN
          ResPageG := PAGE::"Dealer Reserve Entries";

      IF Modal THEN
        PAGE.RUNMODAL(ResPageG, ReservEntry)
      ELSE
        PAGE.RUN(ResPageG, ReservEntry);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE AutoReserve@11(ShowReservationPage@1000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      ReservSetup.GET;
      IF ((("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Quote) AND (ReservSetup."Auto Sales Quote")) OR
         (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Order) AND (ReservSetup."Auto Sales Order")) OR
         (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice) AND (ReservSetup."Auto Sales Invoice")) OR
      // Start INC
         (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Return Order") AND (ReservSetup."Auto Sales Return Order")) OR
      // Stop INC
      // Start PA041510
         (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo") AND (ReservSetup."Auto Sales Credit Memo"))) AND
      // Stop PA041510
         (ReservMgt.SalesLineReservQuantity(Rec,FALSE) > 0)
      THEN BEGIN
        ReservMgt.SalesLineSetReservFor(Rec);
        TESTFIELD("Shipment Date");
        ReservMgt.AutoReserve(
          FullAutoReservation,CALCDATE(ReservSetup."Valid-to Formula","Shipment Date"),'',
          "Shipment Date");
        FIND;
        IF NOT FullAutoReservation AND ShowReservationPage THEN BEGIN
          COMMIT;
          IF CONFIRM(Text022,TRUE) THEN BEGIN
            ShowReservation();
            FIND;
          END;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetDate@22() : Date;
    BEGIN
      IF SalesHeader."Document Type" = SalesHeader."Document Type"::Quote THEN
        EXIT(WORKDATE);
      EXIT(SalesHeader."Posting Date");
    END;

    PROCEDURE Signed@20(Value@1000 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      CASE "Document Type" OF
        "Document Type"::Quote,
        "Document Type"::Order,
        "Document Type"::Invoice,
        "Document Type"::"Blanket Order":
          EXIT(-Value);
        "Document Type"::"Return Order",
        "Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
          EXIT(Value);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ItemAvailability@12(AvailabilityTypeP@1109400000 : 'Date,Variant,Location,Bin');
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      Item.RESET;
      Item.GET("No.");
      Item.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
      Item.SETRANGE("Date Filter",0D,"Shipment Date");

      CASE AvailabilityTypeP OF
        AvailabilityTypeP::Date:
          BEGIN
            Item.SETRANGE("Variant Filter","Variant Code");
            Item.SETRANGE("Location Filter","Location Code");
            Item.SETRANGE("Bin Filter","Bin Code");
            CLEAR(ItemAvailByDate);
            ItemAvailByDate.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            ItemAvailByDate.SETRECORD(Item);
            ItemAvailByDate.SETTABLEVIEW(Item);
            IF ItemAvailByDate.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
              IF "Shipment Date" <> ItemAvailByDate.GetLastDate THEN
                IF CONFIRM(
                   Text012,TRUE,FIELDCAPTION("Shipment Date"),"Shipment Date",
                   ItemAvailByDate.GetLastDate)
                THEN
                  VALIDATE("Shipment Date",ItemAvailByDate.GetLastDate);
          END;
        AvailabilityTypeP::Variant:
          BEGIN
            Item.SETRANGE("Location Filter","Location Code");
            Item.SETRANGE("Bin Filter","Bin Code");
            CLEAR(ItemAvailByVar);
            ItemAvailByVar.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            ItemAvailByVar.SETRECORD(Item);
            ItemAvailByVar.SETTABLEVIEW(Item);
            IF ItemAvailByVar.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
              IF "Variant Code" <> ItemAvailByVar.GetLastVariant THEN
                IF CONFIRM(
                   Text012,TRUE,FIELDCAPTION("Variant Code"),"Variant Code",
                   ItemAvailByVar.GetLastVariant)
                THEN
                  VALIDATE("Variant Code",ItemAvailByVar.GetLastVariant);
          END;
        AvailabilityTypeP::Location:
          BEGIN
            Item.SETRANGE("Variant Filter","Variant Code");
            Item.SETRANGE("Bin Filter","Bin Code");
            CLEAR(ItemAvailByLoc);
            ItemAvailByLoc.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            ItemAvailByLoc.SETRECORD(Item);
            ItemAvailByLoc.SETTABLEVIEW(Item);
            IF ItemAvailByLoc.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
      // Start INC
              IF ("Location Code" <> ItemAvailByLoc.GetLastLocation) AND (ItemAvailByLoc.GetLastLocation <> '') THEN
      // Stop INC
                IF CONFIRM(
                   Text012,TRUE,FIELDCAPTION("Location Code"),"Location Code",
                   ItemAvailByLoc.GetLastLocation)
                THEN
                  VALIDATE("Location Code",ItemAvailByLoc.GetLastLocation());
          END;
        AvailabilityTypeP::Bin:
          BEGIN
            Item.SETRANGE("Variant Filter","Variant Code");
            Item.SETRANGE("Location Filter","Location Code");
            CLEAR(ItemAvailByBin);
            ItemAvailByBin.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            ItemAvailByBin.SETRECORD(Item);
            ItemAvailByBin.SETTABLEVIEW(Item);
            IF ItemAvailByBin.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
      // Start INC
              IF NOT (ItemAvailByBin.GetLastBin IN ['',"Bin Code"]) THEN
      // Stop INC
                IF CONFIRM(
                   Text012,TRUE,FIELDCAPTION("Bin Code"),"Bin Code",
                   ItemAvailByBin.GetLastBin)
                THEN
                  VALIDATE("Bin Code",ItemAvailByBin.GetLastBin);
          END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE BlanketOrderLookup@23();
    BEGIN
      SalesLine2.RESET;
      SalesLine2.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type",Type,"No.");
      SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type"::"Blanket Order");

        SalesLine2.TESTFIELD("Document Type","Document Type"::"Blanket Order");
        "Blanket Order No." := SalesLine2."Document No.";
        VALIDATE("Blanket Order Line No.",SalesLine2."Line No.");
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateDim@26(Type1@1000 : Integer;No1@1001 : Code[20];Type2@1109400001 : Integer;No2@1109400000 : Code[20];Type3@1109400003 : Integer;No3@1109400002 : Code[20];Type4@1109400005 : Integer;No4@1109400004 : Code[20]);
    VAR

    BEGIN

      // Start PA036002.26170
      TableID[2] := Type2;

      // Stop PA036002.27153
      DimMgt.UpdateGlobalDimFromDimSetID("Dimension Set ID","Shortcut Dimension 1 Code","Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetUnitCost@5808();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      GetItem;
      "Qty. per Unit of Measure" := UOMMgt.GetQtyPerUnitOfMeasure(Item,"Unit of Measure Code");

      IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Item THEN
      // Start PA032651
        IF GetItemLocation() THEN
          VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)", ItemLocationG."Unit Cost" * "Qty. per Unit of Measure")
      // Stop PA032651
        ELSE
          VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)",Item."Unit Cost" * "Qty. per Unit of Measure");
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculateUnitCost@5809(ItemLedgEntry@1000 : Record 32) : Decimal;
    VAR
      ValueEntry@1001 : Record 5802;
      CalculatedAdjustedCost@1002 : Decimal;
      ExpectedAdjustedCost@1003 : Decimal;
      UnitCost@1004 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      ValueEntry.RESET;
      ValueEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item Ledger Entry No.",Inventoriable,"Expected Cost");
      ValueEntry.SETRANGE("Item Ledger Entry No.",ItemLedgEntry."Entry No.");
      ValueEntry.SETRANGE(Inventoriable,TRUE);
      IF ItemLedgEntry."Completely Invoiced" THEN
        ValueEntry.SETRANGE("Expected Cost",FALSE);
      IF ValueEntry.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          IF ValueEntry."Expected Cost" THEN
            ExpectedAdjustedCost := ExpectedAdjustedCost + ValueEntry."Adjusted Cost"
          ELSE
            CalculatedAdjustedCost := CalculatedAdjustedCost + ValueEntry."Adjusted Cost";
        UNTIL ValueEntry.NEXT = 0;
      UnitCost :=
        ((ExpectedAdjustedCost / ItemLedgEntry.Quantity *
        (ItemLedgEntry.Quantity - ItemLedgEntry."Invoiced Quantity")) +
        CalculatedAdjustedCost) / ItemLedgEntry.Quantity;
      EXIT(ABS(ROUND(UnitCost * "Qty. per Unit of Measure",0.00001)));
    END;

    PROCEDURE ShowItemChargeAssgnt@5801();
    VAR
      ItemChargeAssgnts@1000 : Page 5814;
      AssignItemChargeSales@1001 : Codeunit 5807;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::"Charge (Item)");
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      TESTFIELD(Quantity);

      ItemChargeAssgntSales.RESET;
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Item Charge No.","No.");
      IF NOT ItemChargeAssgntSales.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
        ItemChargeAssgntSales."Document Type" := "Document Type";
        ItemChargeAssgntSales."Document No." := "Document No.";
        ItemChargeAssgntSales."Document Line No." := "Line No.";
        ItemChargeAssgntSales."Item Charge No." := "No.";
        GetSalesHeader;

        IF ("Inv. Discount Amount" = 0) AND ("Line Discount Amount" = 0 ) AND (NOT SalesHeader."Prices Including VAT") THEN
          ItemChargeAssgntSales."Unit Cost" := "Unit Price"
        ELSE
          IF SalesHeader."Prices Including VAT" THEN
            ItemChargeAssgntSales."Unit Cost" := ROUND(
              (Amount - "Inv. Discount Amount") / Quantity / (1 + "VAT %" / 100),
              Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision")
          ELSE
            ItemChargeAssgntSales."Unit Cost" := ROUND(
              (Amount - "Inv. Discount Amount") / Quantity,
              Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
      END;

      IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
        AssignItemChargeSales.CreateDocChargeAssgn(ItemChargeAssgntSales,"Return Receipt No.")
      ELSE
        AssignItemChargeSales.CreateDocChargeAssgn(ItemChargeAssgntSales,"Shipment No.");
      CLEAR(AssignItemChargeSales);
      COMMIT;

      ItemChargeAssgnts.Initialize(Rec,ItemChargeAssgntSales."Unit Cost");
      ItemChargeAssgnts.RUNMODAL;
      CALCFIELDS("Qty. to Assign");
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateItemChargeAssgnt@5807();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      CALCFIELDS("Qty. Assigned");
      TESTFIELD("Quantity Invoiced","Qty. Assigned");
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.RESET;
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
      IF (CurrFieldNo <> 0) AND (Amount <> xRec.Amount) THEN BEGIN
        ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETFILTER("Qty. Assigned",'<>0');
        IF NOT ItemChargeAssgntSales.ISEMPTY THEN
          ERROR(Text026,
            FIELDCAPTION(Amount));
        ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Qty. Assigned");
      END;

      IF ItemChargeAssgntSales.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN BEGIN
        GetSalesHeader;
        REPEAT
          IF ("Inv. Discount Amount" = 0) AND ("Line Discount Amount" = 0) AND (NOT SalesHeader."Prices Including VAT") THEN BEGIN
            IF ItemChargeAssgntSales."Unit Cost" <> "Unit Price" THEN BEGIN
              ItemChargeAssgntSales."Unit Cost" := "Unit Price";
              ItemChargeAssgntSales.VALIDATE("Qty. to Assign");
              ItemChargeAssgntSales.MODIFY;
            END;
          END ELSE
            IF SalesHeader."Prices Including VAT" THEN BEGIN
              IF ItemChargeAssgntSales."Unit Cost" <> ROUND(
                 (Amount - "Inv. Discount Amount") / Quantity / (1 + "VAT %" / 100),
                 Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision")
              THEN BEGIN
                ItemChargeAssgntSales."Unit Cost" := ROUND(
                  (Amount - "Inv. Discount Amount") / Quantity / (1 + "VAT %" / 100),
                  Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
                ItemChargeAssgntSales.VALIDATE("Qty. to Assign");
                ItemChargeAssgntSales.MODIFY;
              END;
            END ELSE
              IF ItemChargeAssgntSales."Unit Cost" <> ROUND(
                 (Amount - "Inv. Discount Amount") / Quantity,
                 Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision")
              THEN BEGIN
                ItemChargeAssgntSales."Unit Cost" := ROUND(
                  (Amount - "Inv. Discount Amount") / Quantity,
                  Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
                ItemChargeAssgntSales.VALIDATE("Qty. to Assign");
                ItemChargeAssgntSales.MODIFY;
              END;
        UNTIL ItemChargeAssgntSales.NEXT = 0;
        CALCFIELDS("Qty. to Assign");
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DeleteItemChargeAssgnt@5802(DocType@1000 : Option;DocNo@1001 : Code[20];DocLineNo@1002 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETCURRENTKEY(
        "Applies-to Doc. Type","Applies-to Doc. No.","Applies-to Doc. Line No.");
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Type",DocType);
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. No.",DocNo);
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Line No.",DocLineNo);
      IF NOT ItemChargeAssgntSales.ISEMPTY THEN
        ItemChargeAssgntSales.DELETEALL(TRUE);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DeleteChargeChargeAssgnt@5804(DocType@1000 : Option;DocNo@1001 : Code[20];DocLineNo@1002 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF "Quantity Invoiced" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        CALCFIELDS("Qty. Assigned");
        TESTFIELD("Qty. Assigned","Quantity Invoiced");
      END;
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.RESET;
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Type",DocType);
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document No.",DocNo);
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",DocLineNo);
      IF NOT ItemChargeAssgntSales.ISEMPTY THEN
        ItemChargeAssgntSales.DELETEALL;
      // Stop INC
    END;

      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ExitPointCall@5025380(MakeCoddeP@1109400003 : Code[20];TriggerP@1109400002 : Integer;TypeP@1109400001 : Integer;ExitPointIDP@1109400000 : Text[50];VAR EPRecRefP@1109400005 : RecordRef) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(ExitPointUnitG.RunExitPoint(
        ExitPointSetupG."Object Type"::Table,
        DATABASE::"Sales Line",
        MakeCoddeP, TriggerP, TypeP, ExitPointIDP, EPRecRefP, EPRecRef2G, ExitPointParamG));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ExitPoint@5025450(TriggerP@1119452001 : Integer;TypeP@1119432000 : Integer;ExitPointIDP@1119432001 : Text[50]) ReturnR : Boolean;
    VAR
      EPRecRefL@1109400004 : RecordRef;
    BEGIN
      // @ This local function works as ExitPoint wrapper function. It will control the ExitPointCheck function call.
      // @ It passes thru all the handshake parameter values.
      // @ It takes care to provide the processing records as RecordReference to the ExitPointCheck function.
      // @ When possible a Make Code is also identified and passed to the called ExitPointCheck function.

      // Start PA036544
      EPRecRefL.GETTABLE(Rec);
      EPRecRef2G.GETTABLE(xRec);
      ExitPointParamG."Called CurrFieldNo" := CurrFieldNo;
      ReturnR := ExitPointCall("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code", TriggerP, TypeP, ExitPointIDP, EPRecRefL);
      EPRecRefL.SETTABLE(Rec);
      CLEAR(EPRecRef2G);
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SalesLineExitPoint@1101342676(VAR SalesLineP@1101342645 : Record 37;TriggerP@1109400002 : Integer;TypeP@1109400001 : Integer;ExitPointIDP@1109400000 : Text[50]) ReturnR : Boolean;
    VAR
      EPRecRefL@1109400004 : RecordRef;
    BEGIN
      // @ This local function works as ExitPoint wrapper function. It will control the ExitPointCheck function call.
      // @ It passes thru all the handshake parameter values.
      // @ It takes care to provide the processing records as RecordReference to the ExitPointCheck function.
      // @ When possible a Make Code is also identified and passed to the called ExitPointCheck function.

      EPRecRefL.GETTABLE(SalesLineP);
      ReturnR := ExitPointCall(SalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code", TriggerP, TypeP, ExitPointIDP, EPRecRefL);
      EPRecRefL.SETTABLE(SalesLineP);
      CLEAR(EPRecRef2G);
    END;

    BEGIN
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckUserRights@1109400003(ActionTypeP@1109400001 : Integer);
    VAR
      ShowErrorL@1109400000 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'CheckUserRights') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA036544

      // Start INC
      // Start PA033019
      IF "Order Type" <> "Order Type"::Service THEN
        EXIT;
      UserSetupGet();
      CASE Type OF
        Type::" ":
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Change Text" = UserSetupG."Service Change Text"::" ";
        Type::"Account (G/L)":
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service G/L Account Line" = UserSetupG."Service G/L Account Line"::" ";
        Type::Item:
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Item Line" = UserSetupG."Service Item Line"::" ";
        Type::"Charge (Item)":
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Item Line" = UserSetupG."Service Item Line"::" ";
      END;
      IF ShowErrorL THEN
        ERROR(C_INC_YouHaveNoRightsToDoThat,
          SELECTSTR(ActionTypeP + 1, C_INC_InsertModifyDeleteRename),
          TABLECAPTION,
          FIELDCAPTION(Type),
          Type);
      IF (xRec.Type <> Type) AND (ActionTypeP <> ModificationTypeG::Insert) THEN
        CASE xRec.Type OF
          Type::" ":
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Change Text" = UserSetupG."Service Change Text"::" ";
          Type::"Account (G/L)":
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service G/L Account Line" = UserSetupG."Service G/L Account Line"::" ";
          Type::Item:
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Item Line" = UserSetupG."Service Item Line"::" ";
          Type::"Charge (Item)":
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Item Line" = UserSetupG."Service Item Line"::" ";
        END;
      IF ShowErrorL THEN
        ERROR(C_INC_YouHaveNoRightsToDoThat,
          SELECTSTR(ActionTypeP + 1, C_INC_InsertModifyDeleteRename),
          TABLECAPTION,
          FIELDCAPTION(Type),
          xRec.Type);
      // Stop PA033019
      // Stop INC
    END;

      // Start INC
      // Start PA033019
      IF UserSetupG."User ID" = USERID THEN
        EXIT;
      UserSetupG.GET(USERID);
      // Stop PA033019
      // Stop INC
    END;
