    PROCEDURE DiscountOnOptionTable@5025351();
    VAR
      OptionVariantL@1109400000 : Record 5025424;
      TotalSalAmountL@1109400001 : Decimal;
      SalAmountOnLineL@1109400002 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF NOT NotToOptionTableG THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0169755.165049
        OptionVariantL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.","Document Line No.","Document Type",Area);
        OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
        OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
        OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Area, OptionVariantL.Area::Sale);
      // Stop EU.0169755.165049
        OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Type, OptionVariantL.Type::Vehicle, OptionVariantL.Type::"Manuf. Option");
        OptionVariantL.SETFILTER("Unit Price (LCY)",'<>0');
        TotalSalAmountL := 0;
        IF OptionVariantL.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN BEGIN
          REPEAT
            //in case the chaning of the VAT Prod. Posting Group changes the handling of tax
            OptionVariantL."VAT %" := "VAT %";
            IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
              OptionVariantL."Differential Taxation" := TRUE
            ELSE
              OptionVariantL."Differential Taxation" := FALSE;
            OptionVariantL.VALIDATE("Line Discount %", "Line Discount %");
            TotalSalAmountL := TotalSalAmountL + OptionVariantL.Amount;
            OptionVariantL.SetCalculationChange();
            OptionVariantL.MODIFY;
          UNTIL OptionVariantL.NEXT = 0;

          SalAmountOnLineL := Amount;

          IF (SalAmountOnLineL <> TotalSalAmountL) AND OptionVariantL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
            IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
              OptionVariantL.VALIDATE(Amount, SalAmountOnLineL)
            ELSE
              OptionVariantL.VALIDATE(Amount, OptionVariantL.Amount - (SalAmountOnLineL - TotalSalAmountL));
            OptionVariantL.MODIFY;
          END;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE TranslateVehicleStatusField@1109400011(VAR VehicleP@1109400000 : Record 5025400) : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function will translate the Vehicle Status from the Vehicle table into the vehicle Status field in the Sales Line
      // Start INC
      // Start PA032636
      CASE VehicleP."Vehicle Status" OF
        VehicleP."Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle":
          EXIT("Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle");
        VehicleP."Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle":
          EXIT("Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle");
        VehicleP."Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle":
          EXIT("Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle");
        ELSE
      // Start PA041782
          IF ((VehicleP."Vehicle Status" = VehicleP."Vehicle Status"::"Customer Vehicle") AND ("Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle)) OR
             ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"])
          THEN
      // Stop PA041782
            CASE VehicleP."Old Vehicle Status" OF
              VehicleP."Old Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle":
                EXIT("Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle");
              VehicleP."Old Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle":
                EXIT("Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle");
              VehicleP."Old Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle":
                EXIT("Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle");
      // Start PA044649
              VehicleP."Old Vehicle Status"::" ":
                EXIT("Vehicle Status"::" ");
      // Stop PA044649
             END;
      END;
      // Start PA041687
      IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Quote) AND (VehicleP."Vehicle Status" =  VehicleP."Vehicle Status"::"Consignment Vehicle") THEN
          EXIT("Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle");
      // Stop PA041687
      // Start EU.0027334
      IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Quote) AND CheckLocatorResults(VehicleP.VIN) THEN
        EXIT("Vehicle Status");
      // Stop EU.0027334
      ERROR(C_INC015, VehicleP."Vehicle Status");
      // Stop PA032636
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE NoOnLookup@5025353(VAR TextP@1109400000 : Text[250];VAR ItemP@1109400001 : Record 27) ChangedR : Boolean;
    VAR
      StandardTextsL@1109400003 : Record 7;
      GLAccL@1109400004 : Record 15;
      ResourceL@1109400005 : Record 156;
      ServMakeL@1109400006 : Record 5028685;
      GLAccountsListPageL@1109400007 : Page 18;
    BEGIN
      // @ Performs a lookup and fills TextP and buffer records that are passed as parameters by VAR
      // @ TextP - Text[250]
      // @ ItemP - Buffer Record Item
      // @ retval ChangeR - boolean
      // Start INC
      GetSalesHeader();
      // Start PA034531.I001184
      CASE Type OF
        Type::Item:
          BEGIN
            ItemP.SETCURRENTKEY("Item Type","Make Code","No.");
      // Start PA041023
            IF "Order Type" IN ["Order Type"::Service, "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases"] THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA041023
              ServMakeL.GetServiceMakeFilter(SalesHeader."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
              ServMakeL.COPYFILTER("Service Make Code", ItemP."Make Code");
            END ELSE
              IF "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                ItemP.SETFILTER("Make Code",'%1|%2',"Shortcut Dimension 2 Code",'');
                IF IsImporter THEN
                  IF DealerMgmtG.GetDealer() <> '' THEN
                    ItemP.SETRANGE("Make Code","Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
              END;
            CASE "Item Type" OF
              "Item Type"::Vehicle:
                BEGIN
                  IF NOT ItemP.GET(TextP) THEN
                    IF NOT Item.FINDFIRST() THEN
                      ItemP.INIT;
                  IF ItemP.VehModelLookupWithMaster() THEN BEGIN
                    ChangedR := TRUE;
                    TextP := ItemP."No.";
                  END;
                END;

              "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer":
                BEGIN
                  // Start EU.0056036
                  FilterForModelOfVehicle(ItemP);
                  // Stop EU.0056036
                  IF ItemP.GET(TextP) THEN
                    IF NOT Item.FINDFIRST() THEN
                      ItemP.INIT;
                  IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Transfer Fees List", ItemP) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                    TextP := ItemP."No.";
                    ChangedR := TRUE;
                  END;
                END;

              "Item Type"::"Own Option":
                BEGIN
                  IF ItemP.GET(TextP) THEN
                    IF NOT Item.FINDFIRST() THEN
                      ItemP.INIT;
                  IF  PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Own Options List", ItemP) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                    TextP := ItemP."No.";
                    ChangedR := TRUE;
                  END;
                END;
              "Item Type"::Item:
                BEGIN
      // Start EU.0114065
                  IF SalesHeader."General Document" THEN BEGIN
                    ItemP.FILTERGROUP(2);
                    ItemP.SETRANGE("No Inventory Tracking",TRUE);
                    ItemP.FILTERGROUP(0);
                  END;
      // Stop EU.0114065
                  IF ItemP.GET(TextP) THEN
                    IF NOT Item.FINDFIRST() THEN
                      ItemP.INIT;
                  IF ItemP.LookupWithMaster() THEN BEGIN
                    TextP := ItemP."No.";
                    ChangedR := TRUE;
      // Stop PA034531.I001184
                  END;
                END;
            END;
          END;
        Type::"Account (G/L)":
          BEGIN
            IF GLAccL.GET(TextP) THEN
      // Start PA036114.24042
              GLAccountsListPageL.SETRECORD(GLAccL);
      // Start PA036114.24042
            CASE "Order Type" OF
              "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
                GLAccountsListPageL.Def(4);
              "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
                GLAccountsListPageL.Def(5);
              "Order Type"::Service:
                GLAccountsListPageL.Def(6);
            END;
            GLAccountsListPageL.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            IF GLAccountsListPageL.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              GLAccountsListPageL.GETRECORD(GLAccL);
      // Start PA034531.I001184
      // Stop PA034531.I001184
              TextP := GLAccL."No.";
              ChangedR := TRUE;
            END;
            CLEAR(GLAccountsListPageL);
          END;
        Type::" ":
          BEGIN
            IF StandardTextsL.GET(TextP) THEN
              ;
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, StandardTextsL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              TextP := StandardTextsL.Code;
              ChangedR := TRUE;
            END;
          END;
        Type::Resource:
          BEGIN
            IF ResourceL.GET(TextP) THEN
              ;
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, ResourceL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              TextP := ResourceL."No.";
              ChangedR := TRUE;
            END;
          END;
        Type::"Charge (Item)":
          BEGIN
            IF ItemCharge.GET(TextP) THEN
              ;
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, ItemCharge) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              TextP := ItemCharge."No.";
              ChangedR := TRUE;
            END;
          END;
      END;
      IF IsImporter THEN
        IF "Quantity Shipped" <> 0 THEN
          ChangedR := FALSE;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckExclusiveDiffTax@5025355();
    VAR
      VehSalesDiffTaxTextL@1109400000 : Record 5025483;
      VehSalesDocDiffTaxTextL@1109400001 : Record 5025482;
      EnryCounterL@1109400003 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA032651
      // Stop PA032651
      IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN BEGIN
        IF "Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
          ERROR(C_INC024);
        VehSalesDocDiffTaxTextL.RESET;
        VehSalesDocDiffTaxTextL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        VehSalesDocDiffTaxTextL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        IF VehSalesDocDiffTaxTextL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
          GetSalesHeader();
          EnryCounterL := 0;
          VehSalesDiffTaxTextL.RESET;
          VehSalesDiffTaxTextL.SETRANGE("Language Code",SalesHeader."Language Code");
          IF VehSalesDiffTaxTextL.ISEMPTY THEN
            VehSalesDiffTaxTextL.SETRANGE("Language Code",'');
          IF VehSalesDiffTaxTextL.FINDSET THEN
            REPEAT
              VehSalesDocDiffTaxTextL.INIT;
              VehSalesDocDiffTaxTextL."Document Type" := "Document Type";
              VehSalesDocDiffTaxTextL."Document No." := "Document No.";
              EnryCounterL := EnryCounterL + 1;
              VehSalesDocDiffTaxTextL."Entry No." := EnryCounterL;
              VehSalesDocDiffTaxTextL.Text := VehSalesDiffTaxTextL.Text;
              VehSalesDocDiffTaxTextL.INSERT;
            UNTIL VehSalesDiffTaxTextL.NEXT = 0;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE DissolvePurchRelation@5025356();
    VAR
      PurchLineL@1109400000 : Record 39;
      SalesLineL@1109400001 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA041027
      IF "Quantity Shipped" <> 0 THEN
        ERROR(C_INC_CannotBreakRelation, VIN);
      // Stop PA041027
      IF "From Purch. Document No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA041187.92226
        IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0101759.101909
          IF NOT SkipPurchLineUpdateG THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0101759.101909
            PurchLineL.RESET;
            PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "From Purch. Document Type");
            PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "From Purch. Document No.");
            PurchLineL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
            IF PurchLineL.FINDSET THEN
              REPEAT
                PurchLineL."From Sales Document Type" := 0;
                PurchLineL."From Sales Document No." := '';
                PurchLineL."From Sales Line No." := 0;
                IF (VIN <> '') OR (PurchLineL."Line No." = "From Purch. Line No.") OR (PurchLineL."Vehicle Line No." = "From Purch. Line No.") THEN
                  PurchLineL.MODIFY;
              UNTIL PurchLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Start EU.0101759.101909
          END;
      // Stop EU.0101759.101909

          SalesLineL.RESET;
          SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
          SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
          SalesLineL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
            IF SalesLineL.FINDSET THEN
              REPEAT
                SalesLineL."From Purch. Document Type" := 0;
                SalesLineL."From Purch. Document No." := '';
                SalesLineL."From Purch. Line No." := 0;
      // Start EU.0005442.5446
      // Stop EU.0005442.5446
                SalesLineL."Book No." := '';
                SalesLineL."Branch Book No." := '';
                SalesLineL."Serial No." := '';
                IF (VIN <> '') OR (SalesLineL."Line No." = "Line No.") OR (SalesLineL."Vehicle Line No." = "Line No.") THEN
                  SalesLineL.MODIFY;
              UNTIL SalesLineL.NEXT = 0;
        END;
      // Stop PA041187.92226
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE SalesPriceCalculation@5025357();
    VAR
      ItemLedgerEntryL@1109400000 : Record 32;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // When no item was selected, then do not do price calculation
      IF "No." = '' THEN
        EXIT;

      // If no sales line has been created or the quantity is zero, exit
      IF ("Line No." = 0) OR (Quantity = 0) THEN
        EXIT;

      // If a calculation record did already exist, then delete it
      IF OrderItemPriceCalcG.GET(OrderItemPriceCalcG."Order Type"::"Sales Order", "Document Type", "Document No.","Line No.") THEN
        OrderItemPriceCalcG.DELETE;

      // Get item record
      IF Type = Type::Item THEN
        GetItem();

      // Get Standard Sales Price
      IF Type IN [Type::Item,Type::Resource] THEN
        UpdateUnitPrice();

      // Start PA033019.9239993
      // Start EU.0152364.153615
      IF (VIN > '') AND ("Book No." > '') AND("Item Type" IN ["Item Type"::Vehicle,"Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer"]) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0152364.153615
        ItemLedgerEntryL.RESET;
        ItemLedgerEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Variant Code",Open);
        ItemLedgerEntryL.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
      // Start EU.0152364.153615
        ItemLedgerEntryL.SETRANGE("Serial No.",VIN);
        ItemLedgerEntryL.SETRANGE("Book No.", "Book No.");
        ItemLedgerEntryL.SETRANGE("Item Type", "Item Type");
        ItemLedgerEntryL.SETRANGE(Open,TRUE);
        IF NOT ItemLedgerEntryL.FINDFIRST THEN
          IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN
            ItemLedgerEntryL.SETRANGE(Open);
      // Stop EU.0152364.153615
        IF ItemLedgerEntryL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)",CalculateUnitCost(ItemLedgerEntryL));
        END;
      END;
      // Stop PA033019.9239993

      // Start PA037938.51460
      // Stop PA037938.51460

      // Do price calculation for the current sales line
      SalesLinePriceCalcG.SalesPriceCalculation(Rec,SalesHeader,Item,ItemPrice."Allow Price Calculation");

      IF IsImporter() THEN
        IF (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo") AND (DealerMgmtG.GetDealer() <> '')) THEN
          VALIDATE("Line Discount %",xRec."Line Discount %");
      // Start EU.0104306
      IF ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND (VIN > '') THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0104306
        OptionVariantG.RESET;
      // Start EU.0169755.165049
        OptionVariantG.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.","Document Line No.","Document Type",Area);
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Area,OptionVariantG.Area::Sale);
      // Stop EU.0169755.165049
        IF OptionVariantG.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
          REPEAT
            OptionPriceCalcG.SalesPriceCalculation(OptionVariantG, SalesHeader,Rec);
            OptionVariantG.MODIFY;
          UNTIL OptionVariantG.NEXT = 0;
        GetOptionPrice();
      // Start EU.0104306
      END;
      CalcLineInvDiscount();
      // Stop EU.0104306
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalcLineInvDiscount@10430603();
    VAR
      SalShipHeaderL@10430604 : Record 110;
      ShippedSalesHdrL@10430603 : Record 36;
      HdrInvDiscountPercentL@10430602 : Decimal;
      InvDiscountAmountL@10430601 : Decimal;
      OriginalAmountL@10430600 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      SalesSetup.GET;
      IF SalesSetup."Calc. Inv. Discount" THEN
        IF Quantity <> 0 THEN BEGIN
          HdrInvDiscountPercentL := SalesHeader."Inv. Discount %";
          IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice THEN
            IF SalShipHeaderL.GET("Shipment No.") THEN
              IF ShippedSalesHdrL.GET("Document Type"::Order, SalShipHeaderL."Order No.") THEN
                HdrInvDiscountPercentL := ShippedSalesHdrL."Inv. Discount %";
          IF HdrInvDiscountPercentL <> 0 THEN BEGIN
            OriginalAmountL := CalcOriginalAmount(Rec);
            IF "Line Discount %" <> 0 THEN
              OriginalAmountL := OriginalAmountL - ROUND(OriginalAmountL * "Line Discount %" / 100, Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
            InvDiscountAmountL := ROUND(OriginalAmountL * HdrInvDiscountPercentL / 100,0.00001);
            IF InvDiscountAmountL <> "Inv. Discount Amount" THEN BEGIN
              Amount := OriginalAmountL;
              VALIDATE("Inv. Discount Amount", InvDiscountAmountL);
            END;
          END;
        END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalcLineInvDiscountFromAmount@10430602();
    VAR
      SalShipHeaderL@10430603 : Record 110;
      ShippedSalesHdrL@10430602 : Record 36;
      HdrInvDiscountPercentL@10430601 : Decimal;
      InvDiscountAmountL@10430600 : Decimal;
      OriginalAmountL@10430604 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      "Inv. Discount Amount" := 0;
      "Line Discount Amount" := 0;
      IF "Unit Price" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        OriginalAmountL := CalcOriginalAmount(Rec);
        SalesSetup.GET;
        IF SalesSetup."Calc. Inv. Discount" THEN BEGIN
          HdrInvDiscountPercentL := SalesHeader."Inv. Discount %";
          IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice THEN
            IF SalShipHeaderL.GET("Shipment No.") THEN
              IF ShippedSalesHdrL.GET("Document Type"::Order, SalShipHeaderL."Order No.") THEN
                HdrInvDiscountPercentL := ShippedSalesHdrL."Inv. Discount %";
          IF HdrInvDiscountPercentL <> 0 THEN BEGIN
            "Inv. Discount Amount" := ROUND(100 * Amount / (100 - HdrInvDiscountPercentL), 0.00001);
            "Inv. Discount Amount" := ROUND("Inv. Discount Amount" * HdrInvDiscountPercentL / 100, 0.00001);
          END;
        END;
        "Line Discount Amount" := OriginalAmountL - "Inv. Discount Amount" - Amount;
      END;
      IF ("Unit Price" <> 0) AND (OriginalAmountL <> 0) THEN
        "Line Discount %" := ROUND("Line Discount Amount" / OriginalAmountL * 100,0.00001)
      ELSE
        "Line Discount %" := 0;
      IF ABS("Line Discount Amount") < 0.00001 THEN
        "Line Discount %" := 0;
      // Start EU.0138596
      VALIDATE("Autom. Rounding Disc. %", 0);
      // Stop EU.0138596
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckDiscount@5025358();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA040837
      IF CurrFieldNo <> 0 THEN
        IF NOT "Allow Discount" THEN
          IF ("Line Discount %" <> 0) OR ("Quantity Disc. %" <> 0) THEN
            ERROR(C_INC047);
      // Stop PA040837
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE NoOnAssistEdit@5025359() : Boolean;
    VAR
      ItemMasterL@1109400000 : Record 5029101;
      VehicleModelMasterL@1109400001 : Record 5029108;
      ServiceMakeL@1109400002 : Record 5028685;
      ItemMasterPageL@1101353000 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start EU.0174523
      CurrFieldNo := FIELDNO("No.");
      // Stop EU.0174523
      CASE "Item Type" OF
        "Item Type"::Item:
          BEGIN
      // Start PA041023
            IF "Order Type" IN ["Order Type"::Service, "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases"] THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA041023
              ServiceMakeL.GetServiceMakeFilter("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
              ServiceMakeL.COPYFILTER("Service Make Code", ItemMasterL."Make Code");
            END ELSE BEGIN
              IF "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" <> '' THEN
                ItemMasterL.SETRANGE("Make Code", "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
            END;
            ItemMasterPageL := 0;
            IF IsImporter THEN BEGIN
              IF DealerMgmtG.GetDealer() <> '' THEN BEGIN
                DealerSetupG.GET(DealerMgmtG.GetDealer());
                IF NOT DealerSetupG."Allow Item Creation" THEN
                  ERROR(C_IMS000);
                ItemMasterPageL := PAGE::"Dealer Item Master List"
              END;
            END;
      // Start EU.0177226.177535
            IF ItemMasterL.GET("No.", "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code") THEN
              ItemMasterL.INIT;
      // Stop EU.0177226.177535
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(ItemMasterPageL, ItemMasterL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA032651
              "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := ItemMasterL."Make Code";
              VALIDATE("No.", MasterCheckG.CheckMasterRecord(ItemMasterL));
      // Stop PA032651
      // Start PA042000
              EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA042000
            END;
          END;
        "Item Type"::Vehicle:
          BEGIN
            IF "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" <> '' THEN
              VehicleModelMasterL.SETRANGE("Make Code", "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, VehicleModelMasterL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              MasterCheckG.CheckVehicleModel(VehicleModelMasterL);
              "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := VehicleModelMasterL."Make Code";
              VALIDATE("No.", VehicleModelMasterL."No.");
      // Start PA042000
              EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA042000
            END;
          END;
      END;
      // Start PA042000
      EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop PA042000
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertLineNoDistance@5025360(NoOfLinesNeededP@1109400000 : Integer;AbortOnErrorP@1109400001 : Boolean) StepValR : Integer;
    VAR
      ErrorText@1109400002 : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      SalesLine2.RESET;
      SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      SalesLine2 := Rec;
      IF SalesLine2.FIND('>') THEN BEGIN
        StepValR := (SalesLine2."Line No." - "Line No.") DIV (1 + NoOfLinesNeededP);
        IF StepValR = 0 THEN BEGIN
          ErrorText := STRSUBSTNO(C_INC028,
            TABLECAPTION,FIELDCAPTION("Document Type"),"Document Type",FIELDCAPTION("Document No."),"Document No.","Line No.",
            SalesLine2."Line No.");
          IF AbortOnErrorP THEN
            ERROR(ErrorText);
          MESSAGE(ErrorText);
        END;
      END ELSE
        StepValR := 10000;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    END;

        EXIT(FALSE);

      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA036118
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetDepartment@5025364();
    VAR
      LocationL@1109400000 : Record 14;
      PartsDeptL@1109400001 : Record 5028666;
      VehSalesDeptL@1109400002 : Record 5028667;
      ServiceDeptL@1109400003 : Record 5028668;
      VehicleL@1109400004 : Record 5025400;
      GLAccL@1109400005 : Record 15;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA036002.26254
      "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := '';
      // Stop PA036002.26254
      GetSalesHeader();
      IF (Type <> Type::" ") AND ("Location Code" <> '') THEN BEGIN
        LocationL.GET("Location Code");
        CASE "Order Type" OF
          "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
            BEGIN
              PartsDeptL.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
              CASE Type OF
                Type::Item:
                  PartsDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",PartsDeptL."Line Type"::Item);
                Type::"Account (G/L)":
      // Start PA036002.26254
                  BEGIN
                    IF GLAccL.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
                      IF GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code" <> '' THEN
                        "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                     END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
                     PartsDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",PartsDeptL."Line Type"::"G/L Account");
      // Start PA036002.26254
                  END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
                Type::Resource:
                  PartsDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",PartsDeptL."Line Type"::Resource);
                Type::"Charge (Item)":
                  PartsDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type", PartsDeptL."Line Type"::"Charge (Item)");
              END;
      // Start PA036002.26254
              IF  "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" = '' THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA036002.26254
                IF PartsDeptL.FINDFIRST AND (PartsDeptL."Department Code" <> '') THEN
                  "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := PartsDeptL."Department Code"
                ELSE
                  IF (LocationL."Department Code" <> '') THEN
                    "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := LocationL."Department Code"
                  ELSE
                    "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := SalesHeader."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
              END;
      // Start PA036002.26254
            END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
          "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
      // Start PA039974
            BEGIN
              IF VehicleL.GET(VIN) THEN
                "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := VehicleL."Department Code";
      // Stop PA039974
      // Start PA034482
              IF ("Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" = '') OR
                 ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Charge (Item)")
              THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA034482
                VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
                CASE "Item Type" OF
                  "Item Type"::Item:
                    VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehSalesDeptL."Line Type"::Item);
                  "Item Type"::"G/L Account":
      // Start PA036002.26254
                    BEGIN
                      IF GLAccL.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
                        IF GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code" <> '' THEN
                          "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                       END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
                      VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehSalesDeptL."Line Type"::"G/L Account");
      // Start PA036002.26254
                    END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
                  "Item Type"::Vehicle:
                    VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehSalesDeptL."Line Type"::Vehicle);
                  "Item Type"::"Own Option":
                    VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehSalesDeptL."Line Type"::"Own Option");
                  "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer":
                    VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehSalesDeptL."Line Type"::"Veh. Transfer");
                  "Item Type"::"Charge (Item)":
                    VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehSalesDeptL."Line Type"::"Charge (Item)");
                END;
      // Start PA039974
                VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Vehicle Status", "Vehicle Status" - 1);
      // Stop PA039974
      // Start PA036002.26254
                IF "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" = '' THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA036002.26254
                  IF VehSalesDeptL.FINDFIRST AND (VehSalesDeptL."Department Code" <> '') THEN
                    "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := VehSalesDeptL."Department Code"
                  ELSE
                    IF (LocationL."Department Code" <> '') THEN
                      "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := LocationL."Department Code"
                    ELSE
                      "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := SalesHeader."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
      // Start PA036002.26254
                END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
      // Start PA039974
              END ELSE
      // Start PA040739
                IF "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" <> VehicleL."Department Code" THEN
      // Stop PA040739
                  "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := SalesHeader."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
            END;
      // Stop PA039974
          "Order Type"::Service:
            BEGIN
              ServiceDeptL.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
              CASE Type OF
                Type::Item:
                  ServiceDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",ServiceDeptL."Line Type"::Item);
                Type::"Account (G/L)":
      // Start PA036002.26254
                  BEGIN
                    IF GLAccL.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
                      IF GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code" <> '' THEN
                        "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                     END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
                    ServiceDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",ServiceDeptL."Line Type"::"G/L Account");
      // Start PA036002.26254
                  END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
              END;
      // Start PA036002.26254
              IF "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" = '' THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA036002.26254
                IF ServiceDeptL.FINDFIRST AND (ServiceDeptL."Department Code" <> '') THEN
                  "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := ServiceDeptL."Department Code"
                ELSE
                  IF (LocationL."Department Code" <> '') THEN
                    "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := LocationL."Department Code"
                  ELSE
                    "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := SalesHeader."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
      // Start PA036002.26254
              END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
            END;
          ELSE
            "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := SalesHeader."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE VehicleAlreadyInSales@5025365();
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1109400000 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF ("Document Type" <> "Document Type"::Quote) AND
         ("Document Type" <> "Document Type"::"Return Order") AND

        SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Item Type","Item Type"::Vehicle);
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type"::Order, "Document Type"::Invoice);
      // Start PA036650
        IF SalesLineL.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
      // Start EU.0116400.118171
            IF ((SalesLineL."Document Type" <> "Document Type") OR
               (SalesLineL."Document No." <> "Document No.") OR
               (SalesLineL."Line No." <> "Line No.")) AND
               NOT (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo") AND (SalesLineL.Quantity = SalesLineL."Quantity Invoiced"))
      // Stop EU.0116400.118171
            THEN
              ERROR(C_INC023);
          UNTIL SalesLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA036650
      // Stop PA033856
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckMaster@5025366();
    BEGIN
      // Start PA034053.I000514
      GetSalesHeader();
      // Stop PA034053.I000514
      CASE "Item Type" OF
        "Item Type"::Item:
      // Start PA033958
      // Start EU.0210554.215204

          "No." := Item.ItemSearch("No.",SalesHeader."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code", 2, CurrFieldNo);
      // Stop EU.0195242.197191
      // Start PA033958
      // Start PA044817
      // Stop PA044817
      // Stop EU.0210554.215204
      // Stop PA033958
        "Item Type"::Vehicle:
          "No." := Item.VehicleModelSearch("No.",SalesHeader."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
      END;
      IF (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Type)) OR (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("No.")) THEN BEGIN
        IF Type = Type::"Account (G/L)" THEN BEGIN
          CASE "Order Type" OF
            "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":

            "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
              "No." := UserGLAccG.FindGLAccount("No.",UserGLAccG.Area::"Vehicle Sales",USERID);
            "Order Type"::Service:
              "No." := UserGLAccG.FindGLAccount("No.",UserGLAccG.Area::"Service Sales",USERID);
          END;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetOptionPrice@5025368();
    VAR
      OptionVariantL@1109400000 : Record 5025424;
      SalesLineL@1109400004 : Record 37;
      ExRecL@1000 : Record 37;
      SalPriceNewL@1109400001 : Decimal;
      SalAmountNewL@1109400002 : Decimal;
      UnitCostNewL@1109400003 : Decimal;
      SalAmountIncNewL@1109400005 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      IF "Order Type" <> "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start EU.0124939.127063
      IF "Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
      // Stop EU.0124939.127063
        EXIT;
      // Stop EU.0104306
      // Start INC
      SalesLineL.COPY(Rec);
      // Start EU.0169755.165049
      OptionVariantL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.","Document Line No.","Document Type",Area);
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document No.", SalesLineL."Document No.");
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", SalesLineL."Line No.");
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Type", SalesLineL."Document Type");
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Area, OptionVariantL.Area::Sale);
      IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
        OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Type, OptionVariantL.Type::Vehicle);
      IF NOT OptionVariantL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
        OptionVariantL.CALCSUMS("Unit Price", Amount, "Amount Including VAT", "Direct Unit Cost (LCY)");
        SalPriceNewL := OptionVariantL."Unit Price";
        SalAmountNewL := OptionVariantL.Amount;
        SalAmountIncNewL := OptionVariantL."Amount Including VAT";
        UnitCostNewL := UnitCostNewL + OptionVariantL."Direct Unit Cost (LCY)";
      // Start EU.0122714.123474
      // Start EU.0118673
      // Stop EU.0118673
      // Stop EU.0122714.123474
      // Stop EU.0169755.165049
      // Start EU.0104306
        IF GeneralLedgerSetupG.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicInDocActive(SalesHeader."VAT Calculation Logic") THEN
          IF ExRecL.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.") THEN
            IF (ExRecL."Unit Price" <> SalPriceNewL) OR (ExRecL.Amount <> SalAmountNewL) THEN
              SalesLineL.InitManualVAT;
      // Stop EU.0104306
        SalesLineL."Unit Price" := SalPriceNewL;
      // Start EU.0122714.123474
      // Start EU.0118673
      // Stop EU.0118673
      // Stop EU.0122714.123474
        SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)", UnitCostNewL);
        SalesLineL.DefNotToOption(TRUE);
        IF SalesLineL."Unit Price" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
          IF SalesLineL."VAT Calculation Type" <> SalesLineL."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN BEGIN
            SalesLineL."Amount Including VAT" := 0;
            SalesLineL.VALIDATE(Amount, SalAmountNewL);
          END ELSE BEGIN
            SalesLineL.Amount := 0;
            SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Amount Including VAT", SalAmountIncNewL);
          END;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          SalesLineL.Amount := 0;
          SalesLineL."Amount Including VAT" := 0;
        END;
      // Start EU.0104306
        IF GeneralLedgerSetupG.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicInDocActive(SalesHeader."VAT Calculation Logic") THEN
          IF "VAT Amount" <> 0 THEN
            "Amount Including VAT" := Amount + "VAT Amount";
      // Stop EU.0104306
        SalesLineL.DefNotToOption(FALSE);
      END;
      // Start EU.0080873
      // Start EU.0118673
      IF (NOT CalledFromCocpitOptionsG) OR (SalesLineL."Line Discount %" = 0) THEN
      // Start EU.0120161.122112
        IF ("Line Discount %" <> 0) AND ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order", "Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]) THEN
      // Stop EU.0120161.122112
          SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Line Discount %", "Line Discount %");
      // Stop EU.0118673
      // Stop EU.0080873
      COPY(SalesLineL);
      // Stop INC
    END;

      // Start INC

    PROCEDURE IsDepositPosition@5025370();
    BEGIN

      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateFieldInAttachedLines@1055602(UpdateFieldNoP@1055600 : Integer);
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1109400001 : Record 37;
      DepItemMakeSetupL@1101257463 : Record 5205395;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA044975
      IF "Line No." = 0 THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start EU.0091608
      IF STRPOS(DataProcessingOptionsG, '/SkipUpdateFieldInAttachedLines') > 0 THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop EU.0091608
      SalesLineL.RESET;
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      SalesLineL.SETFILTER(Type, '<>%1', Type::" ");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Attached to Line No.", "Line No.");
      IF IsImporter THEN
        SalesLineL.SETFILTER("Additional Item",'%1|%2', SalesLineL."Additional Item"::Deposit, SalesLineL."Additional Item"::"Additional Item");
      IF SalesLineL.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
        REPEAT
          CASE UpdateFieldNoP OF
            FIELDNO(Quantity), FIELDNO("Return Qty. to Receive"), FIELDNO("Qty. to Invoice"), FIELDNO("Qty. to Ship"):
              BEGIN
                IF Quantity = 0 THEN BEGIN
                  SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Qty. to Invoice", 0);
                  SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Qty. to Ship", 0);
                  SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Return Qty. to Receive", 0);
                  IF SalesLineL."Quantity Multiplier" = 0 THEN
                    SalesLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity, SalesLineL."Quantity Shipped")
                  ELSE
                    SalesLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity, 0);
                END ELSE
                  IF (SalesLineL."Quantity Multiplier" <> 0) OR (SalesLineL.Quantity = 0) THEN
                    SalesLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity, AddtlItemG.CalcSalesQty(Quantity, SalesLineL.Quantity, Rec, SalesLineL))
                  ELSE
                    IF IsImporter THEN
                      SalesLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity, 1);
      // Start PA033986
                IF SalesLineL."Quantity Multiplier" <> 0 THEN
                  IF SalesLineL."Additional Item" <> SalesLineL."Additional Item"::" " THEN
                    IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order", "Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
                      SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Return Qty. to Receive", AddtlItemG.CalcSalesQty("Return Qty. to Receive", SalesLineL."Return Qty. to Receive", Rec, SalesLineL));
                IF SalesLineL."Quantity Multiplier" <> 0 THEN
                  IF SalesLineL."Additional Item" <> SalesLineL."Additional Item"::" " THEN
                    IF NOT ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order", "Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]) THEN
      // Start EU.0113943.114335
                      IF SalesLineL."Outstanding Quantity" <> 0 THEN
      // Stop EU.0113943.114335
                        SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Qty. to Ship", AddtlItemG.CalcSalesQty("Qty. to Ship", SalesLineL."Qty. to Ship", Rec, SalesLineL));
                IF SalesLineL."Quantity Multiplier" <> 0 THEN
                  IF SalesLineL."Additional Item" <> SalesLineL."Additional Item"::" " THEN
                    SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Qty. to Invoice", AddtlItemG.CalcSalesQty("Qty. to Invoice", SalesLineL."Qty. to Invoice", Rec, SalesLineL));
              END;
            FIELDNO("Drop Shipment"):
              IF SalesLineL."Additional Item" <> SalesLineL."Additional Item"::" " THEN
                SalesLineL."Drop Shipment" := "Drop Shipment";
      // Stop PA044975
          END;
      // Stop PA033986
          SalesLineL.MODIFY;
        UNTIL SalesLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop INC
      // Start PA035101
      DepItemMakeSetupL.CheckDepositSalesLine(Rec);
      // Stop PA035101

      // Start PA036544
      ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'UpdateAddItemQuantity');
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    PROCEDURE OnDeleteDeleteSubTables@5025373();
    VAR
      ItemPriceCalcL@1109400000 : Record 5025809;
      VarOptL@1109400001 : Record 5025424;
      SalesTradeInL@1109400002 : Record 5025442;
      VehOrderOptInvoiceL@1109400003 : Record 5025464;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start EU.0195242
      IF "Line No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0195242
      // Start EU.0169755.165049
        VarOptL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.","Document Line No.","Document Type",Area);
        VarOptL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
        VarOptL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
        VarOptL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
        VarOptL.SETRANGE(Area, VarOptL.Area::Sale);
      // Stop EU.0169755.165049
      // Start PA036997
        IF NOT VarOptL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
          VarOptL.DELETEALL;
          OptionVariantBOMG.DeleteRecordsFromDocument(VarOptL.Area::Sale, "Document Type", "Document No.", "Line No.");
        END;
      // Stop PA036997
        SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
        IF NOT SalesTradeInL.ISEMPTY THEN
          SalesTradeInL.DELETEALL(TRUE);  //For checking if processed

        IF ItemPriceCalcL.GET(ItemPriceCalcL."Order Type"::"Sales Order", "Document Type","Document No.", "Line No.") THEN
          ItemPriceCalcL.DELETE;
        SalesAssistanceLineG.DeleteDocSalesAssistLine(SalesAssistanceLineG.Area::Sale,"Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");

        IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
          VehOrderOptInvoiceL.RESET;
          VehOrderOptInvoiceL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
          VehOrderOptInvoiceL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
          IF VehOrderOptInvoiceL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            REPEAT
              VehOrderOptInvoiceL.CALCFIELDS("Available in Separate Invoice","Avail. in Separate Posted Inv.");
              IF VehOrderOptInvoiceL."Available in Separate Invoice" THEN
                ERROR(C_INC065,VIN);
              IF (VehOrderOptInvoiceL."Avail. in Separate Posted Inv.") AND ("Quantity Invoiced" <> Quantity) THEN
                ERROR(C_INC065,VIN);
            UNTIL VehOrderOptInvoiceL.NEXT = 0;
            VehOrderOptInvoiceL.DELETEALL;
          END;
        END;
      // Start EU.0195242
      END;
      // Stop EU.0195242
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreatedRelatedLines@5025377(SalesLineP@1109400000 : Record 37) DoPageUpdate : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ Wrapper function for function CreatedRelatedLinesWithStepWidth.
      // @ It will use "0" as LineNoStepWidthP which will make the final additional line creation routine to look for a
      // @ decent step width by itself.
      // Start PA044975
      EXIT(CreatedRelatedLinesWithStepWidth(SalesLineP, 0));
      // Stop PA044975
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreatedRelatedLinesWithStepWidth@1055600(SalesLineP@1109400000 : Record 37;LineNoStepWidthP@1055600 : Integer) DoPageUpdate : Boolean;
    VAR
      TransfExtTextL@1109400001 : Codeunit 378;
      AddItemFuncL@1109400002 : Codeunit 5028716;
    BEGIN
      // @ The function will call the appropriate function in codeunit "Additional Item - Functions"
      // @ It can consider a given Step Width for the Line number creation.
      // Start PA044975
      DoPageUpdate := FALSE;
      IF SalesLineP.Type = SalesLineP.Type::Item THEN
        CASE SalesLineP."Order Type" OF
          SalesLineP."Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
            IF AddItemFuncL.TransferToSales(SalesLineP, LineNoStepWidthP, AddtlItemG.FIELDCAPTION("Consider in Parts Sales")) THEN
              DoPageUpdate := TRUE;
          SalesLineP."Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
            IF AddItemFuncL.TransferToSales(SalesLineP, LineNoStepWidthP, AddtlItemG.FIELDCAPTION("Consider in Vehicle Sales")) THEN
              DoPageUpdate := TRUE;
          SalesLineP."Order Type"::Service:
            IF AddItemFuncL.TransferToSales(SalesLineP, LineNoStepWidthP, AddtlItemG.FIELDCAPTION("Consider in Service Sales")) THEN
              DoPageUpdate := TRUE;
        END;
      IF TransfExtTextL.SalesCheckIfAnyExtText(SalesLineP, FALSE) THEN BEGIN
        TransfExtTextL.InsertSalesExtText(SalesLineP);
      END;
      IF TransfExtTextL.MakeUpdate() THEN
        DoPageUpdate := TRUE;
      // Stop PA044975
    END;

    PROCEDURE DeleteRelatedLines@5025378(WithConfirmationP@1109400000 : Boolean);
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1109400001 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start EU.0091608
      IF ("Line No." <> 0) AND (STRPOS(DataProcessingOptionsG, '/SkipDeleteRelatedLines') = 0) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0091608
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Attached to Line No.", "Line No.");
        SalesLineL.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<>%1', "Line No.");
        IF WithConfirmationP THEN BEGIN
          SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item",SalesLineL."Additional Item"::"Additional Item",SalesLineL."Additional Item"::Deposit);
          IF NOT SalesLineL.ISEMPTY THEN
            IF SalesLineL.COUNT = 1 THEN BEGIN
              IF CONFIRM(C_INC033, TRUE) THEN
                SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item")
              ELSE
                SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item", SalesLineL."Additional Item"::" ");
            END ELSE BEGIN
              IF CONFIRM(C_INC032, TRUE, SalesLineL.COUNT) THEN
                SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item")
              ELSE
                SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item", SalesLineL."Additional Item"::" ");
            END;
        END;
      // Start PA033984
        IF NOT SalesLineL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0089938
          IF SalesLineL.FINDSET THEN
            REPEAT
              IF SalesLineL."Shipment No." = '' THEN
                SalesLineL.TESTFIELD("Qty. Shipped Not Invoiced", 0);
              IF SalesLineL."Return Receipt No." = '' THEN
                SalesLineL.TESTFIELD("Return Qty. Rcd. Not Invd.", 0);
            UNTIL SalesLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop EU.0089938

      // Start PA044975
          SalesLineL.SETFILTER("Reserved Qty. (Base)", '<>0');
          IF SalesLineL.FINDSET THEN
            REPEAT
              SalesHeader.CancelReservationOneLine(SalesLineL);
            UNTIL SalesLineL.NEXT = 0;
          SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Reserved Qty. (Base)");

          SalesLineL.SetDeleteQuietFlag(TRUE);
          SalesLineL.DELETEALL(TRUE);
          SalesLineL.SetDeleteQuietFlag(FALSE);
      // Stop PA044975
        END;
      // Stop PA033984
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item");
        IF NOT SalesLineL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA032441
          SalesLineL.MODIFYALL("Additional Item",SalesLineL."Additional Item"::" ");
          SalesLineL.MODIFYALL("Quantity Multiplier",0);
          SalesLineL.MODIFYALL("Attached to Line No.",0);
        END;
      // Stop PA032441
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE VehOptionShow@5025379();
    VAR
      OptionL@1109400000 : Record 5025424;
      OptionVariantsPageL@1109400001 : Page 5025432;
      DealerOptionVariantsPageL@1116500001 : Page 5086707;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Show Options is only possible for Item Type "Vehicle"
      IF "Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
        MESSAGE(C_INC073,FIELDCAPTION("Item Type"));
        EXIT;
      END;

      OptionL.RESET;
      // Start EU.0169755.165049
      OptionL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.","Document Line No.","Document Type",Area);
      OptionL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
      OptionL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
      OptionL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
      OptionL.SETRANGE(Area, OptionL.Area::Sale);
      // Stop EU.0169755.165049
      IF OptionL.ISEMPTY THEN
        IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
          VehicleUnitG.MakeSalLineOption(Rec);
          COMMIT;
        END;

      GetSalesHeader();
      // Start PA032651
      // Start PA033498.8823967
      // Start PA033733.9231731
      IF IsImporter THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA033733.9231731
        IF DealerMgmtG.GetDealer() > '' THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA033498.8823967
          OptionL.RESET;
          OptionL.FILTERGROUP(2);
          OptionL.SETRANGE(Area, OptionL.Area::Sale);
          OptionL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
          OptionL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
          OptionL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
          OptionL.FILTERGROUP(0);
          CLEAR(DealerOptionVariantsPageL);
          DealerOptionVariantsPageL.SETTABLEVIEW(OptionL);
          DealerOptionVariantsPageL.SETRECORD(OptionL);
          DealerOptionVariantsPageL.EDITABLE(NOT SalesHeader."Dealer Confirmed");
          DealerOptionVariantsPageL.RUNMODAL;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          CLEAR(OptionVariantsPageL);
          OptionVariantsPageL.SETTABLEVIEW(OptionL);
          OptionVariantsPageL.SETRECORD(OptionL);
          IF IsImporter THEN
            OptionVariantsPageL.EDITABLE(NOT SalesHeader."Dealer Confirmed");
      // Stop PA032651
          OptionVariantsPageL.RUNMODAL;
        END;
      // Start PA033733.9231731
      END ELSE BEGIN
        CLEAR(OptionVariantsPageL);
        OptionVariantsPageL.SETTABLEVIEW(OptionL);
        OptionVariantsPageL.SETRECORD(OptionL);
        OptionVariantsPageL.EDITABLE(TRUE);
        OptionVariantsPageL.RUNMODAL;
      END;
      // Stop PA033733.9231731

      IF NOT SalesHeader."Dealer Confirmed" THEN
        GetOptionPrice();
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE LocationCodeAssist@5025384();
    VAR
      ItemLocationL@1109400000 : Record 5028700;
      UserLocationL@1109400002 : Record 5028664;
      LocationFilterL@1109400001 : Text[1024];
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF Type <> Type::Item THEN
        EXIT;
      UserLocationL.SETRANGE("User ID",USERID);
      IF UserLocationL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
      // Start PA032651
          LocationFilterL := LocationFilterL + '|' + UserLocationL."Location Code";
        UNTIL UserLocationL.NEXT = 0;
        LocationFilterL := COPYSTR(LocationFilterL, 2);
      // Stop PA032651
        ItemLocationL.FILTERGROUP(2);
        ItemLocationL.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
        ItemLocationL.SETFILTER("Location Code",LocationFilterL);
        ItemLocationL.FILTERGROUP(0);
      // Start PA036118
        IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, ItemLocationL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
          VALIDATE("Location Code",ItemLocationL."Location Code");
      // Stop PA036118
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE BinCodeOnLookup@1109400025(VAR TextP@1109400000 : Text) : Boolean;
    VAR
      BinL@1109400003 : Record 5400;
      ItemBinL@1109400002 : Record 5028749;
    BEGIN
      // @ Function created to show bins for an Item
      // @ Param TextP returns the value of Bin Code
      // Start PA041146.68559
      TESTFIELD(Type, Type::Item);
      BinL.RESET;
      BinL.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
      IF BinL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          ItemBinL.RESET;
          ItemBinL.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
          ItemBinL.SETRANGE("Location Code",BinL."Location Code");
          ItemBinL.SETRANGE("Bin Code",BinL.Code);
          IF ItemBinL.FINDFIRST THEN
            BinL.MARK(TRUE);
        UNTIL BinL.NEXT = 0;

      BinL.MARKEDONLY(TRUE);
      IF BinL.FINDFIRST THEN
        IF BinL.GET("Location Code", TextP) THEN;
      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::Bins,BinL) <> ACTION::LookupOK THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      TextP := BinL.Code;
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA041146.68559
    END;

    PROCEDURE BinCodeAssist@5025385();

      // Start INC

    END;

    PROCEDURE FindStatus@5025383(SkipLineNoCheckP@1055600 : Boolean);
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1109400000 : Record 37;
      OldStatusL@1109400001 : Integer;
      OldStatusCodeL@1109400002 : Code[20];
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA037802.37581
      IF StatusUpdateDeactivatedG THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA037802.37581
      OldStatusL := "Line Status";
      // Start EU.0090125
      "Line Status" := FindStatus2();
      // Stop EU.0090125
      // Start EU.0095631
      IF SkipLineNoCheckP OR ("Line Status" <> OldStatusL) THEN
      // Stop EU.0095631
        IF SalesLineL.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.") THEN
          MODIFY;
      // Start EU.0090125
      IF NOT NoStatusChangeG THEN
      // Start EU.0174523
        IF NOT SkipUpdateStatusG AND NOT ISTEMPORARY THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0174523
          SalesHeader.GET("Document Type","Document No."); // Force refresh
          OldStatusCodeL := SalesHeader."Status Code";
          IF SkipLineNoCheckP THEN
            SalesHeader.UpdateDocStatus("Line No.")
          ELSE
            SalesHeader.UpdateStatus();
          IF OldStatusCodeL <> SalesHeader."Status Code" THEN
            SalesHeader.MODIFY;
        END;
      // Stop EU.0090125
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE FindStatus2@5025386() : Integer;
    VAR
      DummyDateL@1737401 : Date;
      ReserveQtyOnStockL@1737400 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0095631
      CASE TRUE OF
        "Quantity Invoiced" <> 0:
          IF ("Qty. Shipped Not Invoiced" = 0) AND
             (("Quantity Shipped" = Quantity) OR ("Return Qty. Received" = Quantity))
          THEN
            EXIT("Line Status"::"Completely Invoiced")
          ELSE
            EXIT("Line Status"::"Partly Invoiced");

        ("Quantity Shipped" <> 0) OR ("Return Qty. Received" <> 0):
          IF ("Quantity Shipped" = Quantity) OR ("Return Qty. Received" = Quantity) THEN
            EXIT("Line Status"::"Completely Shipped")
          ELSE
            EXIT("Line Status"::"Partly Shipped");
      // Start EU.0090125
        ELSE
          BEGIN
            IF ("Reserved Quantity" > 0) AND ("Outstanding Qty. (Base)" <> 0) THEN BEGIN
              ReserveQtyOnStockL := CalculateReserveQtyOnStock(DummyDateL);
              IF (ReserveQtyOnStockL <> 0) AND (ReserveQtyOnStockL = "Outstanding Qty. (Base)") THEN
                EXIT("Line Status"::"Fully Reserved on Inventory");
            END;
            IF "Qty. to Ship" > 0 THEN
              EXIT("Line Status"::"Ready for Shipment");
          END;
      END;
      EXIT("Line Status"::" ");
      // Stop EU.0090125
      // Stop EU.0095631
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE StatusCheckFunction@5025387(CheckFieldNumberP@1109400000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF CheckFieldNumberP AND (CurrFieldNo = 0) THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start EU.0104306
      IF CurrFieldNo <> 0 THEN
        IF CurrFieldNo = LastStatusChechOnFieldNoG THEN
          EXIT
        ELSE
          LastStatusChechOnFieldNoG := CurrFieldNo;
      // Stop EU.0104306
      GetSalesHeader();
      SalesHeader.ApplyStatusFunction(FALSE);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckPostingGroup@5025362();
    BEGIN

        IF "Posting Group" = '' THEN
          MESSAGE(C_INC070,VIN);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckBelongingLines@5025390();
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1109400001 : Record 37;
      NextVehLineNoL@1109400000 : Integer;
      NextOtherLineNoL@1109400002 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA039974
      IF "Currency Rounding Position" THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA039974
      IF (VIN = '') AND
         ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND ("Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND
         (Type <> Type::" ") AND (Type <> Type::"Charge (Item)")
      THEN BEGIN
        SalesLine2.RESET;
        SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        SalesLine2.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<%1',"Line No.");
        SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Item Type","Item Type"::Vehicle);
        IF SalesLine2.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
          VIN := SalesLine2.VIN;
          IF SalesLine2.VIN <> '' THEN
            VALIDATE(VIN,SalesLine2.VIN);
          "Vehicle Line No." := SalesLine2."Line No.";
      // Start PA044370
      // Start PA040519
      // Stop PA040519
      // Stop PA044370
        END;
      END;

      IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA037863
        SalesLine2.RESET;
        SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        SalesLine2.SETFILTER("Line No.",'>%1',"Line No.");
        SalesLine2.SETFILTER("No.",'<>%1','');
        SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Item Type","Item Type"::Vehicle);
        IF SalesLine2.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          NextVehLineNoL := SalesLine2."Line No.";
          SalesLine2.SETFILTER("Item Type",'<>%1&<>%2',SalesLine2."Item Type"::Vehicle,SalesLine2.Type::"Charge (Item)");
          IF SalesLine2.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            NextOtherLineNoL := SalesLine2."Line No.";
            IF NextOtherLineNoL > NextVehLineNoL THEN
              EXIT;
          END;
        END;
      // Stop PA037863
        SalesLine2.RESET;
        SalesLine2.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
        SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        SalesLineL.COPY(SalesLine2);
        SalesLine2.SETFILTER("Line No.",'>%1',"Line No.");
        SalesLine2.SETFILTER("No.",'<>%1','');
      // Start PA035482
      // Start PA040553
        SalesLine2.SETFILTER(VIN, '%1|%2', '', xRec.VIN);
      // Stop PA040553
      // Start PA035482
        IF SalesLine2.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
          REPEAT
            IF (SalesLine2."Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND (SalesLine2.Type <> SalesLine2.Type::"Charge (Item)") THEN BEGIN
              SalesLine2.VALIDATE(VIN,VIN);
              IF SalesLine2."Item Type" = SalesLine2."Item Type"::"Own Option" THEN
                IF Item.GET(SalesLine2."No.") AND (Item."Accept posting group from Veh.") THEN BEGIN
                  SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Item Type","Item Type"::Vehicle);
                  IF SalesLineL.FINDFIRST THEN
                    IF NOT (SalesLineL."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLineL."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax") THEN BEGIN
                      SalesLine2.VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group","Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
                      SalesLine2."Posting Group" := VehicleUnitG.FindInvPostGroup(SalesLine2.Type = SalesLine2.Type::Item,
                        SalesLine2."No.",
                        SalesLine2.VIN,
                        SalesLine2."Veh. Opt. Line No.",
                        SalesLine2."Document Type",
                        SalesLine2."Document No.");
                      SalesLine2."VAT Prod. Posting Group" := "VAT Prod. Posting Group";
                    END;
                END;
              SalesLine2."Vehicle Line No." := "Line No.";
              SalesLine2.MODIFY;
            END;
          UNTIL (SalesLine2.NEXT = 0) OR (SalesLine2."Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle);
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckVehicleInsurances@5025391(DeletionP@1109400000 : Boolean);

    PROCEDURE ShowAlternativeParts@1109400000();
    VAR
      SubstItemL@1109400000 : Record 5715;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF Type = Type::Item THEN BEGIN
        SubstItemL.RESET;
        SubstItemL.SETRANGE(Type, SubstItemL.Type::Item);
        SubstItemL.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
        SubstItemL.SETRANGE("Variant Code","Variant Code");
        IF SubstItemL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Alternative Part Entry Lookup",SubstItemL);
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckTaxFromPurchase@5025396();
    VAR
      VehicleL@1109400004 : Record 5025400;
      VATPostingSetupL@1109400003 : Record 325;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA034254.I000942
      IF (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Gen. Prod. Posting Group")) OR (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("VAT Prod. Posting Group")) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA034254.I000942
        IF VehicleL.GET(VIN) THEN BEGIN
          VATPostingSetupL.GET(VehicleL."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)",VehicleL."VAT Prod. Posting Group");
          IF (VATPostingSetupL."VAT Calculation Type" = VATPostingSetupL."VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT") AND
             ("VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax")
          THEN
            ERROR(C_INC025);
      // Stop INC
      // Start PA034254.I000942
        END;
      END;
      // Stop PA034254.I000942
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateServiceOrder@5029396(FieldNoP@1109400000 : Integer);
    VAR
      ServiceLineL@1109400001 : Record 5025625;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF NOT ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Invoice]) THEN
        EXIT;
      IF NOT ServiceLineL.GET(ServiceLineL."Document Type"::Order,"Service Order No.","Service Order Line No.") THEN
        EXIT;

      CASE FieldNoP OF
        FIELDNO("Location Code"):
          IF ServiceLineL."Location Code" = "Location Code" THEN
            EXIT;
        FIELDNO("Shortcut Dimension 1 Code"):
          IF ServiceLineL."Department Code" = "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" THEN
            EXIT;
        FIELDNO("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code"):
          IF ServiceLineL."Make Code" = "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" THEN
            EXIT;
        FIELDNO("Bill-to Customer No."):
          IF ServiceLineL."Bill-to Customer No." = "Bill-to Customer No." THEN
            EXIT;
        FIELDNO("Gen. Bus. Posting Group"):
          IF ServiceLineL."Gen. Bus. Posting Group" = "Gen. Bus. Posting Group" THEN
            EXIT;
        FIELDNO("Gen. Prod. Posting Group"):
          IF ServiceLineL."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" = "Gen. Prod. Posting Group" THEN
            EXIT;
        FIELDNO("Service Posting Group"):
          IF ServiceLineL."Service Posting Group" = "Service Posting Group" THEN
            EXIT;
      END;
      IF FieldG.GET(DATABASE::"Service Line",FieldNoP) THEN
        ERROR(C_INC076,FieldG."Field Caption","Document Type");
      ERROR(C_INC076,FieldNoP,"Document Type");
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckSerialNo@1109400004();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF (VIN <> '') AND ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Own Option") THEN BEGIN
        IF ("Veh. Opt. Line No." = 0) OR
           NOT VehOptionGet(VehicleOptionG, VIN, "Veh. Opt. Line No.") OR
           (VehicleOptionG."Serial No." = '')
        THEN
          TESTFIELD("Serial No.")
        ELSE
          TESTFIELD("Serial No.",VehicleOptionG."Serial No.");
      END ELSE
        IF (VIN <> '') AND ("Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Item) THEN
          TESTFIELD("Serial No.",VIN)
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE VehProtectedCodeShow@1109400002();
    VAR
      VehProtectedCodeL@1109400000 : Record 5045458;
      VehicleL@1109400001 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN

        MESSAGE(C_INC078,FIELDCAPTION("Item Type"));
        EXIT;
      END;
      TESTFIELD(VIN);
      IF NOT VehicleL.GET(VIN) THEN BEGIN
        MESSAGE(C_INC079,VehicleL.TABLECAPTION,FIELDCAPTION(VIN));
        EXIT;

      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE OwnOptionUnitCostGet@1109400006(VAR UnitCostP@1109400001 : Decimal;FieldNoP@1109400000 : Integer;VAR VehOptionFoundP@1109400002 : Boolean) ILEfoundR : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      VehOptionFoundP := FALSE;
      IF (Type <> Type::Item) OR ("Item Type" <> "Item Type"::"Own Option") OR ("No." = '') THEN
        EXIT;
      GetItem();
      UnitCostP := Item."Unit Cost";

      CASE FieldNoP OF
        FIELDNO("Appl.-to Item Entry"):
          ILEfoundR := ItemLedgEntryGet("Appl.-to Item Entry");
        FIELDNO("Appl.-from Item Entry"):
          ILEfoundR := ItemLedgEntryGet("Appl.-from Item Entry");
        FIELDNO("Serial No."):
          BEGIN
            ItemLedgEntry.RESET;
            ItemLedgEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item Type","Item No.",VIN,"Serial No.");
            ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Item Type",ItemLedgEntry."Item Type"::"Own Option");
            ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
            ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);
            ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Serial No.","Serial No.");
            ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Open,TRUE);
            ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Correction,FALSE);
            IF "Location Code" <> '' THEN
              ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
            ILEfoundR := ItemLedgEntry.FINDFIRST;
          END;
      END;
      IF ILEfoundR THEN BEGIN
        ItemLedgEntry.CALCFIELDS("Adjusted Cost");
        UnitCostP := ABS(ItemLedgEntry."Adjusted Cost");
        EXIT;
      END;
      IF "Veh. Opt. Line No." = 0 THEN
        EXIT;
      VehOptionFoundP := VehOptionGet(VehicleOptionG, VIN, "Veh. Opt. Line No.");
      IF NOT VehOptionFoundP THEN
        EXIT;
      UnitCostP := VehicleOptionG."Unit Cost";
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE ItemLedgEntryGet@1109400014(EntryNoP@1109400000 : Integer) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF (EntryNoP = ItemLedgEntry."Entry No.") AND (EntryNoP <> 0) THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      EXIT(ItemLedgEntry.GET(EntryNoP));
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateDescInVehicleOption@1109400007();
    VAR
      VehicleOptionL@1109400000 : Record 5025422;
      VehicleL@1109400001 : Record 5025400;
      VehicleOwnOptL@1109400002 : Record 5045386;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF VehicleOptionL.GET(VIN,"Veh. Opt. Line No.") THEN BEGIN
        VehicleOptionL.Description := Description;
        VehicleOptionL."Description 2" := "Description 2";
        VehicleOptionL.MODIFY;
        VehicleOptionL.UpdateArchiv(2,TRUE,VehicleOptionL.ReturnManual);
      END;

      IF VehicleL.GET(VIN) THEN BEGIN
        VehicleOwnOptL.RESET;
        VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);
        VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Option Code","No.");
        VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Book No.",VehicleL."Current Book No.");
        VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Sales Order No.","Document No.");
        VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Sales Order Line No.","Line No.");
        IF VehicleOwnOptL.FINDFIRST AND (VehicleOwnOptL."Service Order No." = '') AND (VehicleOwnOptL."Option Line No." = 0) THEN BEGIN
          VehicleOwnOptL.Description := Description;
          VehicleOwnOptL."Description 2" := "Description 2";
          VehicleOwnOptL.MODIFY;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE SyncVehicleOwnOption@1109400009(VAR VehicleOwnOptionP@1109400000 : Record 5045386) : Boolean;
    VAR
      VehicleOwnOptL@1109400003 : Record 5045386;
      VehicleL@1109400002 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      VehicleL.GET(VIN);
      VehicleOwnOptL.RESET;
      VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);
      VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Option Code","No.");
      VehicleOwnOptL.SETFILTER("Sales Order Line No.",'<>%1',"Line No.");
      VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Service Order No.", '');
      VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Option Line No.", 0);
      VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Book No.",VehicleL."Current Book No.");
      IF VehicleOwnOptL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        VehicleOwnOptionP."Sales Order No." := VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Order No.";
        VehicleOwnOptionP."Sales Order Line No." := VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Order Line No.";
        VehicleOwnOptL.DELETE(TRUE);
        EXIT(TRUE);
      END;
      EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckOwnOptionPostingGroups@5025405();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC

          END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcItemAvailQty@1119432002(VAR InvAvailableQtyP@1119432001 : Decimal;VAR InvExpectedQtyP@1119432000 : Decimal) InvIsComplAvailableR : Boolean;
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1119432002 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // @ The function should calculate the available quantity of an item depending of the given Location Code and
      // @ should return that the outstanding quantity of an item is completely available.
      // @ param InvAvailableQtyP : Available qty. of an item depending of date filter 0d to eternal and of curr. location.
      // @ param InvExpectedQtyP :  Expected qty. of an item depending of date filter 0d to eternal and of curr. location.
      // @ retval InvIsComplAvailableR : Returns yes if the available quantity is bigger than outstanding qty.
      // Start PA032450
      InvIsComplAvailableR := FALSE;
      InvAvailableQtyP := 0;
      InvExpectedQtyP := 0;
      IF Type <> Type::Item THEN
        EXIT;
      IF "No." = '' THEN
        EXIT;
      IF NOT Item.GET("No.") THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start PA033011.5989972
      IF SalesLineL.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.") THEN BEGIN
        MODIFY;
      // Start PA036852
        COMMIT;
      // Stop PA036852
        SalesLineL := Rec;
      END ELSE
        SalesLineL.INIT;
      // Stop PA033011.5989972
      Item.RESET;
      Item.SETFILTER("Date Filter",'..%1',12319999D);
      Item.SETRANGE("Location Filter","Location Code");
      Item.SETRANGE("Bin Filter","Bin Code");
      InvExpectedQtyP := AvailabilityMgtG.ExpectedQtyOnHand(Item,TRUE,TRUE,0,InvAvailableQtyP,12319999D);
      // Start PA033011.5989972
      // Stop PA033011.5989972
      InvIsComplAvailableR := InvAvailableQtyP + SalesLineL."Outstanding Qty. (Base)" >= "Outstanding Qty. (Base)";
      // Stop PA032450
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitReqWorksheetName@1119432011();
    BEGIN
      // @ The function should initialize the field "Req. Worksheet Name" based on "Requisition Wksh. Name" from Sales Header
      // @ or a specific search using "Purch. Order Type"
      // Start PA032450
      IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases" THEN
        IF (Type = Type::Item) AND ("No." <> '') THEN
      // Start PA041510
          IF ("Req. Worksheet Name" = '') OR (xRec."Location Code" <> "Location Code") OR
             (xRec."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" <> "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code")
          THEN BEGIN
            GetSalesHeader();
            IF (SalesHeader."Requisition Wksh. Name" = '') OR (xRec."Location Code" <> "Location Code") OR
               (xRec."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" <> "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code")
            THEN BEGIN
              VALIDATE("Req. Worksheet Name", ReqWorksheetFunctionsG.GetDefReqWorksheetName(
                SalesHeader."Req. Wksh. Template Name", "Location Code", SalesHeader."Purch. Order Type", "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code", TRUE));
            END ELSE BEGIN
              VALIDATE("Req. Worksheet Name", SalesHeader."Requisition Wksh. Name");
            END;
          END;
      // Stop PA041510
    END;

    PROCEDURE SelectReqWorksheetName@1119432000(VAR ReqWorksheetNameP@1119432001 : Text[1024]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      ReqWorksheetFunctionsL@1119432000 : Codeunit 5028744;
      ReqWorksheetNameL@1119432002 : Code[10];
    BEGIN
      // @ Here a filtered lookup for field "Req. Worksheet Name" is provided by calling a function in codeunit
      // @ "Req. Worksheet Functions".
      // @ param ReqWorksheetNameP : Contains the current or the selected new value of field "Req. Worksheet Name".
      // @ retval : Returns true if the user has selected a new value.
      // Start PA032450
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      ReqWorksheetNameL := ReqWorksheetNameP;
      // Start PA032651
      IF NOT ReqWorksheetFunctionsL.SelectReqWorksheetName(ReqWorksheetNameL,'',"Location Code","Shortcut Dimension 2 Code","No.") THEN
      // Stop PA032651
        EXIT(FALSE);
      ReqWorksheetNameP := ReqWorksheetNameL;
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA032450
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckMakecodeConsistent@1119432003() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ Check that Make Code is same as corresponding item/vehicle.
      // @ retval - Boolean
      // Start PA032651.6147260
      IF CurrFieldNo <> FIELDNO("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code") THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF (Type <> Type::Item) THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      CASE "Item Type" OF
        "Item Type"::Vehicle:
          BEGIN
            IF VIN <> '' THEN BEGIN
              VehicleG.GET(VIN);
              IF ("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" <> VehicleG."Make Code") AND (VehicleG."Make Code" <> '') THEN BEGIN
                "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := VehicleG."Make Code";
                IF GUIALLOWED THEN
                  ERROR(C_INC_MakeConsistentVeh,FIELDCAPTION("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code"),VIN,"Item Type");
              END;
            END;
            IF "No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
              GetItem;
              IF ("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" <> Item."Make Code") AND (Item."Make Code" <> '') THEN BEGIN
                "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := Item."Make Code";
                IF GUIALLOWED THEN
                  ERROR(C_INC_MakeConsistentModel,FIELDCAPTION("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code"),"No.")
              END;
            END;
          END;
        "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer":
          BEGIN
            IF "No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
              GetItem;
              IF ("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" <> Item."Make Code") AND (Item."Make Code" <> '') THEN BEGIN
                "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := Item."Make Code";
                IF GUIALLOWED THEN
                  ERROR(C_INC_MakeConsistentVeh,FIELDCAPTION("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code"),"No.","Item Type")
              END;
            END;
          END;
        "Item Type"::"Own Option":
          BEGIN
            IF "No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
              GetItem;
              IF ("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" <> Item."Make Code") AND (Item."Make Code" <> '') THEN BEGIN
                "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := Item."Make Code";
                IF GUIALLOWED THEN
                  ERROR(C_INC_MakeConsistentVeh,FIELDCAPTION("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code"),"No.","Item Type")
              END;
            END;
          END;
        ELSE
          EXIT(TRUE);
      END;
      // Stop PA032651.6147260

      // Start PA035597
      UpdateDimSetID();
      // Stop PA035597
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckNegativeStock@1119432001();
    VAR
      ReservationEntryL@1119432003 : Record 337;
      ItemJnlCheckLineL@1119432000 : Codeunit 21;
      ReservationMgtL@1119432002 : Codeunit 99000845;
      ReservedQtyOnInvL@1119432001 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // @ The function has to prepare some data to call the real function in codeunit 21.
      // Start PA032800
      IF CurrFieldNo <> FIELDNO("Qty. to Ship") THEN
        EXIT;
      IF (Type <> Type::Item) OR ("Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Item) OR
         ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Quote,"Document Type"::"Credit Memo","Document Type"::"Return Order"]) OR
         ("Qty. to Ship" = 0)
      THEN
        EXIT;
      IF "Reserved Qty. (Base)" <> 0 THEN
        ReservedQtyOnInvL := ReservationMgtL.CalcReservQtyOnInventory(
          ReservationEntryL."For Type"::Sales,"Document Type","Document No.","Line No.",'',"No.","Location Code","Bin Code");
      IF ItemJnlCheckLineL.CheckNegItemStockAllowed(
         "No.","Location Code","Bin Code",USERID,"Qty. to Ship (Base)",ReservedQtyOnInvL,GETPOSITION(TRUE))
      THEN
        EXIT;
      "Qty. to Ship" := xRec."Qty. to Ship";
      // Stop PA032800
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckReplacement1toN@1100409000() : Boolean;
    VAR
      CurrentItemReplacementsL@1100409000 : Record 5028701;
    BEGIN
      // @ checks if for this added Item No. an 1 to N Replacement was stored into Current Item Replacements Table.
      // Start PA033958
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.RESET;
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("Old Item No.","No.");
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("1:N Replacement",TRUE);
      IF NOT CurrentItemReplacementsL.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop PA033958
    END;

    PROCEDURE Fill1toNReplIntoPurchLines@1100409002() : Code[20];
    VAR
      CurrentItemReplacementsL@1100409000 : Record 5028701;
      SalesLineL@1100409001 : Record 37;
      NewLineNoL@1100409002 : Integer;
      ReplacedItemNoL@1100409003 : Code[20];
      RetItemNoL@1100409004 : Code[20];
    BEGIN
      // @ Fill 1 to N Repl Into Purch Lines
      // Start PA033958
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.RESET;
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("Old Item No.","No.");
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("1:N Replacement",TRUE);
      IF CurrentItemReplacementsL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        ReplacedItemNoL := "No.";
        "No." := CurrentItemReplacementsL."New Item No.";
        RetItemNoL := "No.";
      // Start PA036118
        CurrentItemReplacementsL.NEXT;
        REPEAT
          SalesLineL.INIT;
          SalesLineL := Rec;
          SalesLineL."Line No." := SalesLineL.GetNextLineNo();
      // Stop PA036118
          SalesLineL.VALIDATE("No.",CurrentItemReplacementsL."New Item No.");
          SalesLineL.INSERT;
        UNTIL CurrentItemReplacementsL.NEXT = 0;
        CurrentItemReplacementsL.RESET;
        CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("Old Item No.",ReplacedItemNoL);
        CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("1:N Replacement",TRUE);
        IF NOT CurrentItemReplacementsL.ISEMPTY THEN
          CurrentItemReplacementsL.DELETEALL;
      END ELSE
        RetItemNoL := "No.";
      EXIT(RetItemNoL);
      // Stop PA033958
    END;

    PROCEDURE AdditionalItemQtyConfirmation@1101368192() : Boolean;

      END;
      // Stop PA033986
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcSalesIncentives@1101286982(HideDialogP@1101286983 : Boolean);
    VAR
      SalesHdrL@1101286982 : Record 36;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA033985.19040
      CLEAR(SalesIncentiveMgmtG);
      SalesHdrL.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
      SalesIncentiveMgmtG.SetHideConfirmMsg(HideDialogP);
      SalesIncentiveMgmtG.UpdateSalesIncentivesSale(SalesHdrL,Rec);
      SalesIncentiveMgmtG.SetHideConfirmMsg(FALSE);
      // Stop PA033985.19040
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateDimSetID@1109400018();
    BEGIN
      // Start PA037802.37581
      IF SkipDimensionUpdateG THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA037802.37581
      // Start PA035597
      IF ("Dimension Set ID" = 0) OR
         (LastDimCodesG <> "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" + '/' + "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code")
      THEN BEGIN
        ValidateShortcutDimCode(1,"Shortcut Dimension 1 Code");
        ValidateShortcutDimCode(2,"Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
      END;
      LastDimCodesG := "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" + '/' + "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code";
      // Stop PA035597
    END;
