    PROCEDURE CheckForLineDuplicates@1109400019();
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1109400000 : Record 37;
      AdditionalItemL@1109400003 : Record 5028716;
      LineTypeTextL@8524400 : Text;
      AddItemDuplicateWarningBufferL@1055600 : Text;
      CounterL@1055603 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // @ Function checks for duplicated lines on documents with type Order.
      // Start PA037942
      UserSetupGet;
      CASE UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No." OF
        UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::" ":
          EXIT;
        UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::Warning,
        UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::Error:
          BEGIN
      // Start EU.0004860
            LineTypeTextL := FORMAT(Type);
            IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
              LineTypeTextL := FORMAT("Item Type");
      // Stop EU.0004860
            SalesLineL.RESET;
            SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
            SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
            SalesLineL.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<>%1',"Line No.");
            SalesLineL.SETRANGE(Type,Type);
            SalesLineL.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
      // Start PA044975
      // Start EU.0004860
            SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Item Type", "Item Type");
            IF NOT SalesLineL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
              IF UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No." = UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::Error THEN
                ERROR(C_INC_DuplicateError,LineTypeTextL,"No.");
              IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC_DuplicateWarning, FALSE, LineTypeTextL,"No.") THEN
                ERROR('');
      // Stop EU.0004860
            END;
      // Start PA037942.48468
            AdditionalItemL.RESET;
            AdditionalItemL.SETRANGE("Additional Item No.","No.");
            CASE "Order Type" OF
              "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
                AdditionalItemL.SETRANGE("Consider in Parts Sales", TRUE);
              "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
                AdditionalItemL.SETRANGE("Consider in Vehicle Sales", TRUE);
              "Order Type"::Service:
                AdditionalItemL.SETRANGE("Consider in Service Sales", TRUE);
            END;
      // Start EU.0053218
            IF AdditionalItemL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
              IF UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No." = UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::Error THEN
                ERROR(C_INC_DuplicateErrorAddItem, Type, "No.");
              REPEAT
                CounterL += 1;
                AdditionalItemL.CALCFIELDS("Item Description");
                AddItemDuplicateWarningBufferL :=  AddItemDuplicateWarningBufferL + '\' +
                  STRSUBSTNO('%1. %2 %3', CounterL, AdditionalItemL."Item No.", AdditionalItemL."Item Description");
              UNTIL AdditionalItemL.NEXT = 0;
              IF NOT CONFIRM(STRSUBSTNO(C_INC_DuplicateWarningAddItem, Type, "No.", AddItemDuplicateWarningBufferL, '\\'),FALSE) THEN
                ERROR('');
            END;
      // Stop EU.0053218
      // Stop PA044975
          END;
      // Stop PA037942.48468
      END;
      // Stop PA037942
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckCodedPart@1109400023();
    BEGIN
      // @ function to check if Coded Part values can be deleted
      // @ and clear the "Coded Part Identifier"
      // Start PA040667
      IF (xRec.Type <> Rec.Type) OR (xRec."No." <> "No.") THEN BEGIN

        CodedPartValG.DeleteCodedValues("Serial No.", "No.");
      // Stop PA040070.63485
      // Start PA040867
        "Serial No." := '';
      // Stop PA040867
      END;
      // Stop PA040667
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ClearFieldsInLinkedPurchase@1109400026();
    VAR
      PurchaseLineL@1109400000 : Record 39;
      PurchaseLine2L@1109400001 : Record 39;
    BEGIN
      // @ Clears the "From Sales.." fields in the linked purchase lines.
      // Start PA040026
      IF "From Purch. Document No." = '' THEN
        EXIT;
      PurchaseLineL.SETRANGE("From Sales Document Type", "Document Type");
      PurchaseLineL.SETRANGE("From Sales Document No.", "Document No.");
      PurchaseLineL.SETRANGE("From Sales Line No.", "Line No.");
      IF PurchaseLineL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          PurchaseLine2L.GET(PurchaseLineL."Document Type",PurchaseLineL."Document No.",PurchaseLineL."Line No.");
          PurchaseLine2L."From Sales Document Type" := PurchaseLine2L."From Sales Document Type"::Quote;
          PurchaseLine2L."From Sales Document No." := '';
          PurchaseLine2L."From Sales Line No." := 0;
          PurchaseLine2L.MODIFY(TRUE);
        UNTIL PurchaseLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA040026
    END;

    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckEmmisionLegalTxt@1000009901();
    VAR
      EmissionRelevantLegalTextL@1109400000 : Record 5205862;
      EmissionDocRlvntLegalTextL@1109400001 : Record 5205861;
      EnryCounterL@1109400003 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // @ Reads Setup and creates emission related Legal Text
      // Start PA042665
      EmissionDocRlvntLegalTextL.RESET;
      EmissionDocRlvntLegalTextL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      EmissionDocRlvntLegalTextL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");

        GetSalesHeader();
        EnryCounterL := 0;
        EmissionRelevantLegalTextL.RESET;
        EmissionRelevantLegalTextL.SETRANGE("Language Code",SalesHeader."Language Code");

          EmissionRelevantLegalTextL.SETRANGE("Language Code",'');

            EmissionDocRlvntLegalTextL."Document No." := "Document No.";

            EmissionDocRlvntLegalTextL."Entry No." := EnryCounterL;
            EmissionDocRlvntLegalTextL.Text := EmissionRelevantLegalTextL.Text;
            EmissionDocRlvntLegalTextL.INSERT;
          UNTIL EmissionRelevantLegalTextL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // Stop PA042665
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateReservedLinesFromSales@1055603();
    VAR
      RequisitionLineL@1055600 : Record 246;
      PurchLineL@1055601 : Record 39;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function will update the Reserved Req.Line and Purchase Line "Supply VIN" Values.

      // Start PA041023
      IF Signed("Quantity (Base)") < 0 THEN BEGIN
        ReservMgt.InitFilterAndSortingLookupFor(ReservEntry,TRUE);
        ReservMgt.SalesLineFilterReservFor(ReservEntry,Rec);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        ReservMgt.InitFilterAndSortingLookupFrom(ReservEntry,TRUE);
        ReservMgt.SalesLineFilterReservFrom(ReservEntry,Rec);
      END;
      // Start PA041023.87192
      IF ReservEntry.FINDFIRST THEN;
      // Stop PA041023.87192
      // Start PA041023.87291
      IF ReservEntry."From Type" = ReservEntry."From Type"::"Requisition Line" THEN
      // Stop PA041023.87291
        IF RequisitionLineL.GET(ReservEntry."From ID", ReservEntry."From Batch Name", ReservEntry."From Ref. No.") THEN BEGIN
          RequisitionLineL.VALIDATE("Supply VIN", "Supply VIN");
          RequisitionLineL.VALIDATE("Reference License No." ,"Reference License No.");
          RequisitionLineL.MODIFY;
        END;
      // Start PA041023.87291
      IF ReservEntry."From Type" = ReservEntry."From Type"::Purchase THEN
      // Stop PA041023.87291
        IF PurchLineL.GET(PurchLineL."Document Type"::Order, ReservEntry."From ID", ReservEntry."From Ref. No.") THEN BEGIN
          IF PurchLineL."Cockpit Entry No." <> 0 THEN
            ERROR(C_INC_CockpitEntryCreated);
          PurchLineL.VALIDATE("Supply VIN", "Supply VIN");
          PurchLineL.VALIDATE("Reference License No.", "Reference License No.");
          PurchLineL.MODIFY;
        END;
      // Stop PA041023
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculateReserveQtyOnStock@36900(VAR FirstReservationDateP@1737400 : Date) QuantityR : Decimal;
    VAR
      ResEntryL@36902 : Record 337;
      ReservMgtL@36901 : Codeunit 99000845;
    BEGIN
      // @ This is a support function to calculate the sum of Quantity on Reservation Entries from stock (From Type = Item Ledger Entry) linked to the line
      // @ param FirstReservationDateP : "Creation Date" of the first reservation related to the line
      // @ retval : Decimal with the calculated Quantity
      // Start EU.0000369
      // Start EU.0017374
      FirstReservationDateP := 0D;
      // Stop EU.0017374
      IF "Reserved Quantity" = 0 THEN
        EXIT(0);
      ReservMgtL.InitFilterAndSortingLookupFor(ResEntryL, TRUE);
      ReservMgtL.SalesLineFilterReservFor(ResEntryL, Rec);
      // Start EU.0017374
      // Note "From Type" is empty in case of reservation on no inventory tracking item
      ResEntryL.SETFILTER("From Type", '%1|%2', ResEntryL."From Type"::" ", ResEntryL."From Type"::"Item Ledger Entry");
      ResEntryL.CALCSUMS(Quantity);
      QuantityR := ResEntryL.Quantity;
      IF QuantityR > 0 THEN
        IF ResEntryL.FINDFIRST THEN
          FirstReservationDateP := ResEntryL."Creation Date";
      // Stop EU.0017374
      // Stop EU.0000369
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateTempReplChain@1055604(ItemNoP@1055600 : Code[20];ChainNoP@1055601 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      // @ This function creates records in a temporary Replacement Chain Record to display replacements
      // @ that have not yet been completed.
      // @ param ItemNoP - Code 20
      // @ param ChainNoP - Integer

      // Start PA044817
      ReplcmtChainTempG.INIT;
      ReplcmtChainTempG."Item No." := ItemNoP;
      ReplcmtChainTempG."Chain No." := ChainNoP;
      IF ReplcmtChainTempG.INSERT THEN
        ;
      // Stop PA044817
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckItemReplcmnt@1055608();
    VAR
      CurrItemReplL@1055600 : Record 5028701;
      CurrItemRepl2L@1055603 : Record 5028701;
      ReplChainL@1055601 : Record 5028707;
      ReplChain2L@1055602 : Record 5028707;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function searches, according to Item Replacement Status, for uncomplete replacements in
      // @ Current Item Replacement table.

      // Start PA044817
      IF Item."Replacement Status" = Item."Replacement Status"::"Will be replaced" THEN BEGIN
        CurrItemReplL.RESET;
        CurrItemReplL.SETRANGE("Old Item No.", "No.");
        IF CurrItemReplL.FINDSET THEN
          // Handle N to 1 future replacements
          IF CurrItemReplL."N:1 Replacement" THEN BEGIN
            // Found the first of the line
            IF CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No." = 0 THEN BEGIN
              CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."Old Item No.",1);
              CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."New Item No.",1);
              // Search for the attached
              CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
              CurrItemRepl2L.SETCURRENTKEY("Attached to Replacement No.");
              CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Attached to Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Replacement No.");
              IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDSET THEN
                REPEAT
                  CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."Old Item No.",1);
                UNTIL CurrItemRepl2L.NEXT = 0;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              // Found an attached replacement, so find the first in line
              CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
              CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No.");
              IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."Old Item No.",1);
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."New Item No.",1);
              END;
              // Search for the attached
              CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
              CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Attached to Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No.");
              IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDSET THEN
                REPEAT
                  CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."Old Item No.",1);
                UNTIL CurrItemRepl2L.NEXT = 0;
            END;

          END ELSE BEGIN
            // This may handle both 1:1 or 1:N current replacements
            REPEAT
              CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."Old Item No.",1);
              CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."New Item No.",1);
            UNTIL CurrItemReplL.NEXT = 0;
          END;
      END ELSE
        IF Item."Replacement Status" = Item."Replacement Status"::"Replacement Item" THEN BEGIN
          CurrItemReplL.RESET;
          CurrItemReplL.SETRANGE("New Item No.", "No.");
          IF CurrItemReplL.FINDSET THEN
            // Handle 1 to N future replacements
            IF CurrItemReplL."1:N Replacement" THEN BEGIN
              // Found the first of the line
              IF CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No." = 0 THEN BEGIN
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."Old Item No.",1);
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."New Item No.",1);
                // Search for the attached
                CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
                CurrItemRepl2L.SETCURRENTKEY("Attached to Replacement No.");
                CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Attached to Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Replacement No.");
                IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDSET THEN
                  REPEAT
                    CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."New Item No.",1);
                  UNTIL CurrItemRepl2L.NEXT = 0;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                // Found an attached replacement, so find the first in line
                CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
                CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No.");
                IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                  CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."Old Item No.",1);
                  CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."New Item No.",1);
                END;
                // Search for the attached
                CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
                CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Attached to Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No.");
                IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDSET THEN
                  REPEAT
                    CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."New Item No.",1);
                  UNTIL CurrItemRepl2L.NEXT = 0;
              END;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              // This may handle both 1:1 or N:1 current replacements
              REPEAT
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."Old Item No.",1);
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."New Item No.",1);
              UNTIL CurrItemReplL.NEXT = 0;
            END;
        END;
      // Stop PA044817
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckLocatorResults@1055605(VinP@1055600 : Code[20]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      VehSearchResultL@1055601 : Record 5205930;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function searches the Vehicle Search Results for the VIN on the other companies

      // Start EU.0027334
      VehSearchResultL.SETRANGE(VIN, VinP);
      VehSearchResultL.SETFILTER("Company Name",'<>%1', COMPANYNAME);
      VehSearchResultL.SETFILTER("Vehicle Status",'<>%1',VehSearchResultL."Vehicle Status"::"Customer Vehicle");
      IF VehSearchResultL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        CASE VehSearchResultL."Vehicle Status" OF
          VehSearchResultL."Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle":
            "Vehicle Status":= "Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle";
          VehSearchResultL."Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle":
            "Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle";
          VehSearchResultL."Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle":
            "Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle";
          VehSearchResultL."Vehicle Status"::"Consignment Vehicle":
            "Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status"::"Consigment Vehicle";
        END;
        EXIT(TRUE);
      END ELSE
        EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0027334
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitManualVAT@124();
    BEGIN
      // @ This function inizialize the VAT field in record

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ConfirmItemReplacement@4729401();
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0047294
      IF NOT IsImporter THEN BEGIN
        IF Item.GET("No.") THEN
          CASE Item."Replacement Status" OF
            Item."Replacement Status"::"Has been replaced":
              ShowReplcmtG := CONFIRM(C_INC039,TRUE,"No.");
            Item."Replacement Status"::"Replacement Item":
              ShowReplcmtG := CONFIRM(C_INC052,TRUE,"No.");
            Item."Replacement Status"::"Will be replaced":
              BEGIN
                ShowReplcmtG := CONFIRM(C_INC038,TRUE,"No.");
                FutureReplG := TRUE;
              END;
          END;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        RequireSelectionG := FALSE;
        IF "No." = Item."No." THEN
          CASE Item."Replacement Status" OF
            Item."Replacement Status"::"Has been replaced":
              BEGIN
                // Use avail Inventory before allowing replaced Item use.
                IF NOT ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Order,"Document Type"::Invoice]) THEN
                  ShowReplcmtG := CONFIRM(C_INC039,TRUE,"No.")
                ELSE BEGIN
                  Item.CALCFIELDS(Inventory,"Qty. on Order/Invoice");
                  IF (Item.Inventory - Item."Qty. on Order/Invoice" + "Outstanding Qty. (Base)") <= 0 THEN BEGIN
                    MESSAGE(C_IMS002,"No.");
                    RequireSelectionG := TRUE;
                    ShowReplcmtG := TRUE;
                  END;
                END;
              END;

            Item."Replacement Status"::"Replacement Item":
              //Check all old replaced Inventory used first.
              IF NOT ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Order,"Document Type"::Invoice]) THEN
                ShowReplcmtG := CONFIRM(C_INC052,TRUE,"No.")
              ELSE BEGIN
                ReplcmtChainG.RESET;
                ReplcmtChainG.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
                IF ReplcmtChainG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                  ReplcmtChain2G.RESET;
                  ReplcmtChain2G.SETCURRENTKEY("Chain No.");
                  ReplcmtChain2G.SETRANGE("Chain No.",ReplcmtChainG."Chain No.");
                  ReplcmtChain2G.SETFILTER("Item No.",'<>%1',"No.");
                  IF ReplcmtChain2G.FINDSET THEN
                    REPEAT
                      IF Item2G.GET(ReplcmtChain2G."Item No.") AND
                          (NOT Item2G.Blocked) AND
                          (Item2G."Replacement Status" = Item2G."Replacement Status"::"Has been replaced")
                      THEN BEGIN
                        Item2G.SETRANGE("Location Filter",SalesHeader."Location Code");
                        Item2G.CALCFIELDS(Inventory,"Qty. on Order/Invoice");
                        IF (Item2G.Inventory - Item2G."Qty. on Order/Invoice" + "Outstanding Qty. (Base)") > 0 THEN BEGIN
                          MESSAGE(C_IMS003);
                          RequireSelectionG := DealerMgmtG.GetDealer() <> '';
                          ShowReplcmtG := TRUE;
                        END;
                      END;
                    UNTIL (ReplcmtChain2G.NEXT = 0) OR RequireSelectionG;
                END;
              END;

            Item."Replacement Status"::"Will be replaced":
              IF Item."Old Replacement Status" = Item."Old Replacement Status"::"Replacement Item" THEN
                ShowReplcmtG := CONFIRM(C_INC052,TRUE,"No.");
          END;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0047294
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ReValidateItemNoField@2542300(NewItemNoP@2542301 : Code[20]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      OldItemL@2542300 : Record 27;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0025423
      IF "No." = NewItemNoP THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      OldItemL.GET("No.");
      // Stop EU.0000048.6892
      WithoutReplcmtWindowG := TRUE;
      VALIDATE("No.", NewItemNoP);
      WithoutReplcmtWindowG := FALSE;
      // Start EU.0042147.40362
      IF OldItemL."Replacement Status" IN [OldItemL."Replacement Status"::"Has been replaced",OldItemL."Replacement Status"::"Will be replaced"] THEN
        "Order Manuf. Item No." := OldItemL."No.";
      // Stop EU.0042147.40362
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0025423
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE FilterForModelOfVehicle@5603600(VAR ItemP@5603601 : Record 27);
    VAR
      SalesLineL@5603600 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // @ This Function is used to filter the Item for the Model of the associated Vehicle line
      // Start EU.0056036
      IF "Order Type" <> "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
        EXIT;
      IF "Item Type" <> "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer" THEN
        EXIT;
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
      IF VIN = '' THEN
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Line No.", "Vehicle Line No.")
      ELSE
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      IF SalesLineL.FINDFIRST THEN
          ItemP.SETFILTER("Model Code",'%1|%2', SalesLineL."No.", '');
      // Stop EU.0056036
    END;

    PROCEDURE SelectOwnOptions@5603601() : Boolean;
    VAR
      ItemL@5603603 : Record 27;
      ModelL@5603602 : Record 27;
      SalesLineL@5603601 : Record 37;
      OwnOptionsListL@5603600 : Page 5025495;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function is used to select multiple Own Options
      // Start EU.0056036
      IF "Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      IF ModelL.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
        ItemL.FILTERGROUP(2);
        ItemL.SETRANGE("Item Type", ModelL."Item Type"::"Own Option");
        ItemL.SETRANGE("Make Code", ModelL."Make Code");
        IF ModelL."Vehicle Category Code" <> '' THEN
          ItemL.SETFILTER("Vehicle Category Code", '%1|%2', ModelL."Vehicle Category Code", '');
        ItemL.SETFILTER("Model Code", '%1|%2', OwnOptionsListL.GetModelFilter(Rec), '');
        ItemL.FILTERGROUP(0);
        OwnOptionsListL.SETTABLEVIEW(ItemL);
      END;
      OwnOptionsListL.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);

      IF OwnOptionsListL.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
        OwnOptionsListL.SETSELECTIONFILTER(ItemL);
        IF ItemL.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            SalesLineL.INIT;
            SalesLineL."Document No." := "Document No.";
            SalesLineL."Document Type" := "Document Type";
            SalesLineL."Line No." := SalesLineL.GetNextLineNo();
            SalesLineL.Type := Type::Item;
            SalesLineL.SetValidateAvailableQty(TRUE);
            SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Item Type", SalesLineL."Item Type"::"Own Option");
            SalesLineL.VALIDATE("No.", ItemL."No.");
            SalesLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity, 1); // Set "Qty. to Ship" and "Qty. to Invoice"
            SalesLineL."Vehicle Line No." := "Line No.";
            SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Unit Price", ItemL."Unit Price");
            SalesLineL.INSERT(TRUE);
          UNTIL ItemL.NEXT = 0;
        EXIT(TRUE);
      END;
      EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0056036
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE IsOrderLinkedWithQuote@10435700() : Boolean;
    VAR
      DocChainEntryL@10435700 : Record 5206330;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104357.106191
      GetSalesHeader;
      IF SalesHeader."Document Chain No." = 0 THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);

      DocChainEntryL.SETRANGE("Chain No.",SalesHeader."Document Chain No.");
      DocChainEntryL.SETRANGE("Document Type",DocChainEntryL."Document Type"::"Vehicle Quote");
      EXIT(NOT DocChainEntryL.ISEMPTY);
      // Stop EU.0104357.106191
    END;

                             Amount Rounding process restructured. With help of the new RunOrderLineRounding and UpdateVATAmountRounding functions the Amount Rounding process
                             is called only in the end of the first Amount influencing code trigger. Before it was called several times even from other triggers.
